  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa aw, nangmah ah ka ginna ka koih jel hi; chikmah chiangin zahlakin honomsak ken.</li>
      <li>Na diktatna vangin honhumbitin, honhonkhia inla: kei lamah na bil hondohin, honhondam in.</li>
      <li>Kei dingin omna suangpi, ka hohtheih gigena ding, hong hiin: nang honhondam dingin thu na pia a; ka suangpi leh ka kulhpi na hi ngala.</li>
      <li>Ka Pathian aw, mi gilou- salou khut akipan honhonkhia in, mi diktatlou leh nunsia khut akipan.</li>
      <li>Toupa Pathian aw, nang ka lamet na hi ngala: ka naupan chik akipan ka hon muan na hi hi.</li>
      <li>Ka nu gil akipan him in nangmah kaihin ka om jela: ka nu sung akipan honlakhepa na hi: nangmah ahi, ka honphat gige ding.</li>
      <li>Mitampi theihin thillamdang kahi a; himahleh nang ka kihumbitna kiptak na hi.</li>
      <li>Ka kam nang phatna in a dim ding, nitumin na pahtawinain a dim ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka tek chiangin honpaikhe kenla, ka tha a jawt chiangin hon paisan ken.</li>
      <li>Ka melmaten ka tungtangthu a gen ngal ua; ka hinna tangte leng a kikou uhi.</li>
      <li>Pathianin a paisanta: delh unla, man un; humbitpa ding himhim a om ngal keia chiin.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, hon gamlat mahmah ken: ka Pathian aw, honpanpih dingin kin in.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna tunga melmate zahlak leh mangthangin om uhenla; ka siatna ding zongte gensiatna leh zumnaa khuhin om uhen.</li>
      <li>Himahleh ken jaw ka lamen gige dinga, ka honphat semsem ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka kamin na diktatna thu a gen ding a, nitumin ka hotdamna thu a gen dinga: a tamdan ka thei ngal keia.</li>
      <li>Toupa Pathian thilhih thupiakte toh ka hongpai ding a: a diktatna, nangmah diktatna thu kia, ka gen ding hi.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, ka naupan chik akipan nang non hilha; tu tanin na thillamdang hihte ka theisak gige hi.</li>
      <li>A hi, Pathian aw, ka teka ka sam a kan hun inleng hon paisan mahmah ken; na hatna tuh khangthak nawnte kiangah leh, na thilhihtheihna hongom lai dingte kianga ka theihsak mateng.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, na diktatna leng a sang mahmah ahi; Pathian aw, nang thil thupitakte hihpa, nangmah bang kua a om?</li>
      <li>Nang, buaina tampi leh thupitak honmusakpan non hingsak nawn dinga, lei thukpi akipan non pi khe nawn ding hi.</li>
      <li>Nang ka thupina honhihkhangsak inla, hongkihei nawn inla, hon khamuan in.</li>
      <li>Pekgingin leng ka hon phat dinga, ka Pathian aw, na thutak ngei ka phat ding. Nang Israelte Mi Siangthou aw, kaihging toh nangmah phatin la ka sa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Nangmah phata la ka sak chiangin ka muk a nuam mahmah dinga; ka hinna na tat mah leng a nuam mahmah ding hi.Ka leiin leng nitumin na diktatna thu a gen ding; ka siatna ding zongte a zahlak un a zumta ngal ua.</li>
      <li>Ka leiin leng nitumin na diktatna thu a gen ding; ka siatna ding zongte a zahlak un a zumta ngal ua.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian aw, na vaihawmnate kumpipa kiangah pia inla, na diktatna kumpipa tapa kiangah pia in.</li>
      <li>Na mite tuh diktatnain vai a hawmsak dinga, na mi gentheite tuh vaihawmna dikin vai a hawmsak ding hi.</li>
      <li>Tanglian leh tangneu ten diktatnain mite kiangah khamuanna a hontun ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Aman mi laka gentheite tuh vai a hawmsak dinga, tagah tate tuh a hondam dinga, nuaisiahpa bel a hihjan ding hi.</li>
      <li>Tunga ni a om sungin a kikou ding ua, kha om sungin leng, suan om sung tengteng inleng.</li>
      <li>Amah tuh loupa gawitan tunga vuah kia bangin a ke dinga; lei vak vuah tui bang maiin.</li>
      <li>A damlai un mi dikte tuh a pha luahluah ding uh, huan, khamuanna thupidan, kha om louh masiahin.</li>
      <li>Aman tuipi akipana tuipi dang phain leng thu a nei ding, luipi akipan kawlmong phain leng.</li>
      <li>Gamdaia omte tuh a maah a kun ding ua: a melmaten leng leivui a liak ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Tarsis gam leh tuikulh gam kumpipaten kipahman a hontawi ding ua; Sheba leh Seba gam kumpipaten thilpiakte a honlan ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Ahi, kumpipa tengteng tuh a maah a khupboh ding ua: nam chitengin a na a sem ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Gentheiin a sap chiangin aman a humbit dinga, mi tagah, panpihpa neilou leng a humbit ding hi.</li>
      <li>Mi genthei leh tagahte a hehpih dinga, tagahte hinna a hondam ding hi.</li>
      <li>A hinna uh tuh nuaisiahna leh hiamgamna lak akipan a tan dinga, a sisan uh amah ngaihdan in manpha tak ahi ding ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Huan, a hing ding ua; Sheba gam dangkaeng akipana piak ahi dinga: miten amah a thumsak gige ding uhi; nitumin vual a jawlsak ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Leiah, mualvum peuhah, buh tampi a om dinga; a vui tuh Lebanon bangin a ling suausuau dinga, khuaa mite bel loupa bangin a pha lihliah ding uhi.</li>
      <li>A min tuh khantawnin a om tawntung dinga; a min tuh ni a om sungin tatlak louin a om jel dinga; mite tuh amah ah vualjawl in a om ding ua; nam chih ten amah tuh hampha a chi ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Toupa Pathian, Israelte Pathian phatin om hen, amah kiain thillamdang a hih jela.</li>
      <li>A min thupi tak khantawnin phatin leng om henla; lei pumpi leng a thupinaa hihdimin om hen. Amen, Amen.Jesai tapa David thumnate a beita hi.</li>
      <li>Jesai tapa David thumnate a beita hi.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian tuh Israelte tungah a nahoih ngei e, lungtang siangthoute tunga.</li>
      <li>Himahleh ken jaw ka siktal dekdeka; ka kalsuante a teu dekdek ahi.</li>
      <li>Mi gilou-saloute vangphatdan ka muhin mi mangte ka eng ngala.</li>
      <li>A sih lai un thuakna himhim a neikei ua: a hatna u tuh a kip zosop ngala.</li>
      <li>Mi dang banga gimthuakin a om kei uhi. Midang banga gawtin leng a om sam kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin kisaktheihnain khainiang bangin a ngawng uh a vela; hiam gamnain puansilh bangin a tuam hi.</li>
      <li>Thau jiakin a mit uh a pawng leulaw u a: lungtang thudeih sanga thupi a nei uhi.</li>
      <li>A nuihsan ua, giloutakin nuaisiahna thu a gen ua: kisaktheihnain a pau uhi.</li>
      <li>A kam uh van khawngah a koih ua, a lei un leitung a pha suak jel hi.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin a mite tuh huaiah a kik nawn ua. Tui nou-a dim tuh amau dawn siang sipsipin om hi.</li>
      <li>Pathianin bangchin a thei dia? Tungnungpenin theihna a nei dia hia? a chi ua.</li>
      <li>En dih, hiaite khawng mi gilou-saloute ahi uhi; nuamsa taka om gigein a hau deuhdeuh jel uhi.</li>
      <li>A thawn maiin ahi, ka lungtang ka hihsiana, ka khutte gensiatbeia ka sil.</li>
      <li>Nitumin gawtin ka oma, jingsang tengin sawiin ka om ngala.</li>
      <li>Huchi bangin ka gen ding, na chitaleng; ngaidih, taka hih ka na hi ding.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh ka theihtheihna dingdan ka ngaituahin, Keia dingin a na lua ahi.</li>
      <li>Pathian mun siangthou a ka luta, a beina ding uh ka ngaituah masiah.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh mun nal takahte na koih ngeia; siatna ahte khawng na pai khe jel hi.</li>
      <li>Bangchidan ahia mitphiat kal kiaa a ingam tak u aw! thil mulkimhuai taktea hihmanthat vekin a omta uhi.</li>
      <li>Min khanloh nunga mang bangmah a sak louh bang un, Toupa aw, na halh hunin amau lim leng bangmah na sa kei ding hi.</li>

      <li>Himahleh na kiangah ka om gige a: ka khut taklam na len gige hi.</li>
      <li>Nang na lemtheihnain non pi dinga, huai nung chiangin thupina ah non kipahpih ding hi.</li>
      <li>Van ah nang lou ngal kua ka neia? Lei ah leng nang lou ngal ka deih kuamah a om kei hi.</li>
      <li>Ka sa leh ka lungtang a bahta a: himahleh Pathian tuh khantawna ka lungtang utna ding leh ka tantuan ding ahi.</li>
      <li>Ngaiin, nangmah gamlata omte a mangthang dek ua: a hon angkawmsan peuhmahte tuh na hihmangta ahi.Kei adingin bel Pathian naih a hoiha: Toupa Pathian tuh ka kihumbitnain ka neia, na nasep tengteng thu ka hilh theihna dingin.</li>

      <li>Pathian aw, bangdinga honpai mang den ding na hia oi? Bangdinga na gantatna muna belamte tunga na hehna a khut?</li>

      <li>A giahna mun tak uah a ke saka, a omna buk kim khawng uah.</li>

      <li>Huan, a mun siangthou gamgi a pi tunga, hiai tang, a khut taklama a lei.</li>

      <li>Belampu nou kaite zuihna akipanin a pi khiaa, a mite Jakobte leh a gouluah ding Israelte vak dingin.Huchiin aman a lungtang uh hoihna bangjelin amaute a vaka; khut siamin a pita hi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian aw, nam chih na gouluah dingah a lut ua; na biakin siangthou hihnin ua; Jerusalem suang chim a vum uhi.</li>
      <li>Na sikhate luang tuh tungleng vasate an dingin a pia ua, na mi siangthoute sa tuh gamsate kiangah a pia ua.</li>
      <li>A sisan uh Jerusalem kimah tui bangin a sung bua ua; amau vui ding lah kuamah a om ngal kei ua.</li>
      <li>I kim ua mite gensiatin I na om ua, I kiangnai khawnga mite muhsit leh nuihsatin I naom ta uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, bangtan ahia na heh nilouhlouh ding? Na mullitna tuh mei bangin a kuang ding ahia?</li>
      <li>Nangmah theilou nam chih tungah na hehna sung buain, na min kou gam tungahte khawng leng.</li>
      <li>Jakobte tuh a ne khin ua; a omna uh a hihgamta ngal ua.</li>
      <li>Ka pipute uh thulimlouhnate ka lak uah theigige ken: na lainatnain honnadon pah hen. Nakpitaka hihniamin ka omta ngal ua.</li>
      <li>Honhondampa Pathian aw, na min thupina dingin honpanpih inla; na min jiakin honbumbit inla, ka khelhnate uh sil siangin.</li>
      <li>Bangachia nam chihin, A Pathian uh koia om ahia leh? Na sikhate sisan pawt phulakna ka mitmuh un nam chih lakah theih hi hen.</li>
      <li>Henta thumna na maah tung hen: na thilhihtheihna thupidan bang jelin si dinga sehte tuh humbit inla:</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang a hon gensiatna uh, ka kiangnai uate tungah aleh sagih veiin thuk in.Huchiin, kou na mite, na gan tatna muna belamten, khantawnin kipahthu ka honhilh ding uhi: suan tengteng tanin nangmah phatna tuh ka theisak jel ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchiin, kou na mite, na gan tatna muna belamten, khantawnin kipahthu ka honhilh ding uhi: suan tengteng tanin nangmah phatna tuh ka theisak jel ding uhi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Israelte chingpa, Belam pawl banga Josephte pipa, bil na doh in: nang cherubte tunga tu, hongvak khia in.</li>
      <li>Ephraimte leh Benjaminte leh Manasite mitmuhin na hatna tokthou inla, honhondam dingin hongpai in.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, honkihei sak nawn inla; na mel hihvak in, huchiinhotdamin ka om ding uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, sepaihte Pathian, bangtan ahia na mite thumna tunga na heh ding?</li>
      <li>Amaute khitui-tanghouin na vaka, khitui dawn dingin tehna lian takin na pe jel hi.</li>
      <li>Nang ka kim ua mite adingin kinakna din non bawl naka: ka melmate uh a nui chiat nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Sepaihte Pathian aw, honkihei sak nawn inla: na mel hihvak in, huchin hotdamin ka om ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Aigupta gam akipan grep gui na honla a: nam chih na delh khiaa, na suanta hi.</li>
      <li>A ma na hih siang jela, thutakin zung a kaia, gam tuh a luah vek hi.</li>
      <li>Tangte a lim tuamin a om chiat, ahiangte Pathian sidar singte bang hial ahi.</li>
      <li>A hiangte tuh tuipi tanin a jam suak saka a selte Luipi phain.</li>
      <li>Bangachia a huangte hihsia na hia? Lampi a pai peuhmahin a sat kheta uhi.</li>
      <li>Gamnuaia ngalin a hihsia a, gamsaten leng a ne uhi.</li>
      <li>Sepaihte Pathian aw, hehpih takin kihei nawnin; van akipanin honensuk inla, hiai grep gui en inla, hongveh in.</li>
      <li>A kung na khut taklamin a suan leh, ahiang nang dia na khauhsak toh.</li>
      <li>Mei ah a kangta, phukin a omta: na mela salhna jiakin a mangthang jel hi.</li>
      <li>Na taklama mi tungah na khut om hen, mihing tapa nang dia na hihhat tungah.</li>
      <li>Huchiin kon kiksan kei ding ua: honhihhalh inla, huchiin na minka lou ding hi.TOUPA aw, sepaihte Pathian, hon kihei sak nawn inla; na mel hihvak in. huchiin hotdamin ka om ding uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, sepaihte Pathian, hon kihei sak nawn inla; na mel hihvak in. huchiin hotdamin ka om ding uhi.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian honhihhatpa pahtawiin nuamtakin lasa unla; Jakobte Pathian pahtawin nuam takin kikou un.</li>
      <li>Phatna lasa unla, khuangnou te, kaihging ngaihnophuaite, pekging te toh hontawi un.</li>
      <li>Kha thakin pengkul mut unla, kha lika I ankuangluina thupi niin.</li>
      <li>Israelte dinga thuseh ahi ngala, Jakobte Pathian dan ahi.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh Joseph te laka thutheihsakna dingin a seh ahi. Aigupta gam tunga a pai khiak laiin: ka theihlouh pau ka jak laiin.</li>
      <li>A liangjang thil gik akipanin ka lasuana: a khutte loh akipana khahin a om hi.</li>
      <li>Mangbatniin non sama, ka honhumbita; van ging bukna munah ka hon dawnga; Meribah tuiahte khawng ka hon zeet ahi. Selah</li>
      <li>Ka mite aw, ngaikhia unla, ka hontheihsak bangin; Israelte aw, ka thu ngaikhe nuamle uteh aw!</li>
      <li>Gam dang Pathian himhim na lak uah a om ding uh ahi keia; mi dang Pathian himhim na biak ding uh leng ahi kei hi.</li>
      <li>Kei, TOUPA na Pathian uh ka hi a, Aigupta gam akipan honpi khepa tak: na kam uh lian kat unla, ka hihdim ding ahi.</li>
      <li>Himahleh ka miten ka aw a ngaikhe sam kei ua; Israelten hon deih kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchiin a lungtang uh genhakdan bang jela om dingin ka khahzamta ahi, amau hoihsak banga a om na ding un.</li>
      <li>Aw, ka miten ka thu ngaikhiain, Israelte ka lampi-ahte pai le u aw:</li>
      <li>A melmate uh ka hihneu zokin, amau galte tungah ka khut ka lik ding hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA hote a kiangah a kipe lut ding uhi; amau hun bel a om nilouhlouh ding ahi.Nou bel buh hoihpenin kon vak ding hi; suangpi-a khuaijuin ka hontaisak ding ahi.</li>
      <li>Nou bel buh hoihpenin kon vak ding hi; suangpi-a khuaijuin ka hontaisak ding ahi.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian tuh Pathian kikhopna bawlah a dinga; Pathiante lakah vai ahawm hi.</li>
      <li>Bangtan ahia diklou taka vai na hawm ua, mi gilou-saloute, na deihsak tuam ding uh? Selah</li>
      <li>Gentheite leh paneiloute vai tuh hawm unla; haksa thuakte leh tagahte tungah hihdik un.</li>
      <li>Gentheite leh tagahte gum unla; migilousalou khut akipan humbit un.</li>
      <li>A theikei ua, theihsiamna leng a neikei uh; mialah a kileh a kileh ua: leilung kingakna tengteng tuh a lingta a.</li>
      <li>Pathiante na hi ua, na vek un Tungnungpen tate na hi ua, ka chi hi.</li>
      <li>Himahleh mihingte bang phetin na hongsi ding ua, mi lian khat bangin na hongpuk ding uhi.Pathian aw, thou inla, lei vai hawmsak in: nam chih na gouluah ding ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, thou inla, lei vai hawmsak in: nam chih na gouluah ding ahi ngala.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian aw, paulou in om kenla: Pathian aw, dai nilouh ken, om maimai mahmah ken.</li>
      <li>Ngaiin, nangmah melmate a lum lutlut ua: nangmah hote a dak hawkhawk uhi.</li>
      <li>Na mite lepchiahtakin a sawm ua, na mi selgukte tungah a selamin a kihou a kihou khawm uhi.</li>
      <li>Kisa dih ua, a nam uh mangsak khopin i hihmang ding uh: Israel min himhim theihgigea a om nawn louhna dingin, a chi ua.</li>
      <li>Thu khat satin a kihou ua; na tungah a selama hih dingin thu a kichiam khawm uhi.</li>
      <li>Edomte leh Israelte puan innte, Moabte leh Haggarte;</li>
      <li>Gebalte leh Ammonte leh Amelekte; Philistiate Tura khuaa omte toh:</li>
      <li>Assuriate leng amau lamah a pang sam ua; Lot suante tuh a panpih uhi. Selah</li>
      <li>Amau tuh Midiante tunga na hih bangte, Kison luia Sisera tunga na hih bangte, Jabin tunga na hih bangtein hih sam in.</li>
      <li>Huai mite tuh Endor khua ah a mang ua; lei adingin eklei bang lel a na hita uhi.</li>
      <li>A miliante uh Oreb leh Zeeb bangin bawl inla, ahi, a kumpipate tengteng uh Zebah leh Zalmunna bangin bawl in.</li>
      <li>Huai miten, Pathian omnate I luah sak ding uh, a chi ua.</li>
      <li>Ka Pathian aw, amaute tuh leivui kipei lunglung bangin bawlin: buhsi huih mutleng uakuak bang lelin.</li>
      <li>Gam kang mei bang leh, tang kang meikuang bangin.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh na huihpiin delh inla, na huih thupi takin hihlau in.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na min a zon theihna ding un a mel uh zumnain hihdimin.</li>
      <li>Khahtawnin zahlak leh mangbang takin om uhenla; ahi, hihzuma omin mangthang uhen.Nangmah kia tuh Jehovah minpu, leitung tengteng tunga Tungnungpen na hi chih a theihna ding un.</li>
      <li>Nangmah kia tuh Jehovah minpu, leitung tengteng tunga Tungnungpen na hi chih a theihna ding un.</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Sepaihte TOUPA aw, na omnate deihhuai natel e!</li>

      <li>A hi, kawlgitin in a mu a, lensiamin leng amaha adingin bu a mu a, a nou koihna dingin sepaihte TOUPA aw, ka Kumpipa leh ka Pathian, huai tuh nangmah maitamte ngei ahi hi.</li>
      <li>Na inn a omten nuam a sa ua; nang a honphat gige ding uhi, Selah.</li>
      <li>Nangmaha hatnanei min nuam a sa hi; a lungtanga Zion naihna lamliante om in.</li>
      <li>Kahna guam tuh a tot un, tuikhuk omnate a bawl ua, ahi, vuahtui ke masain vualjawlnain a khuh lel hi.</li>
      <li>Hatna akipanin hat nawn semna ah a pai ua, Zion ah Pathian maah a kimusak chiat uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, Sepaihte Pathian, ka thumna hon ngaikhia inla: Jakobte Pathian aw, bil na dohin. Selah.</li>
      <li>Pathian ka phaw pen u aw, enin, na thaunilhpa mel enin.</li>
      <li>Na biakin huang sung intuala ni khat om tuh mun danga ni sang khat sangin a hoihzo ngala. Gitlouhna puaninte-a om sangin I Pathian ina kongkhakngak hih leng ka ut jaw ahi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA Pathian tuh ni leh phaw ahi ngala: TOUPAN hehpihna leh thupina a pe dinga: diktaka omte lakah thil hoih himhim a it kei ding hi.Sepaihte TOUPA aw, nangmah muang min nuam asa hi.</li>

      <li>TOUPA, na gam tungah na kipaka: Jakobte, sala a om utuh na pi kik nawnta ahi.</li>

      <li>Na thangpaihna tengteng tuh na la manga: na hehna thupitak na kiheisanta hi.</li>
      <li>Honhondampa Pathian aw, honkihei sak nawn inla, ka tung ua na hehna tuh tawpsak in.</li>

      <li>Nangmaha na mite a kipah theihna ding un non hihhalh nawn kei dia hia?</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na chitna tuh honmu sak inla, na hotdamna leng honpia in.</li>
      <li>TOUPA Pathian thu gen dingka ngaikhe ding: a mite leh a mi siangthoute kiangah khamuanna thu a gen dek ngala: himahleh amau tuh haina lamah kihei nawnta kei uhen.</li>
      <li>A hotdamna tuh amah kihtate naihin a om ngeingei nak hi; I gam ua thupina a om theihna dingin.</li>
      <li>Chitna leh thutak a kituak a; diktatna leh kituahna a kitawpa,</li>
      <li>Thutak tuh lei akipanin a dawn khiaa; diktatnain van akipanin a hontan sukta hi.</li>
      <li>Ahi, TOUPAN thil hoih a pe dinga; I gamin leng a thilpou a pe ding hi.Diktatnain ama a kai dinga; a khapte tuh lampi-ah a siam ding hi.</li>

      <li>TOUPA aw, honhehpih inla; nitumin ka honsam ngala.</li>
      <li>Na sikha hinna hihnuam in; TOUPA aw, ka lungsim na kiangah ka koih det jiakin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA, nang, na hoiha, ngaihdam na ngapa, a honsam peuhmah tungah chitna na hau ngal hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, ka thumna ah na bil na dohin; hehpih kon ngetna aw ngaikhia in.</li>
      <li>Ka mangbatna niin kon sam dinga a, lah non dawng ding hi,</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, pathiante lakah nang bang himhim a om kei ua; na thilhihte bang thilhih himhim leng a om kei hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na siam nam chihte a hongpai ding ua, na maah a hongkun ding ua, na min a honpahtawi ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Nang na thupi ngala, thillamdangte leng na hihjela; nangmah kia Pathian na hi hi.</li>

      <li>TOUPA ka Pathian aw, ka lungtang tengtengin ka honphat dinga; na min khantawnin ka pahtawi ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka tunga na chitna a thupi jiakin, ka hinna kokhuk nuainungpen akipan na humbit ngala.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, mi kisatheiten honsual ua, mi ngongtat omkhawmten ka hinna hihmang tumin a zong ua, nang tuh a ma uah a honkoih kei nak uhi.</li>

      <li>Keilam hongnga inla, aw, honhehpihin, na sikha kiangah na hatna pia inla, na sikhanu ta hondam in.Hoihna ding chiamtehna honlak in; honhoten huai tuh a muh ua, a zahlakna ding un, TOUPA, nang non panpih-a, non khamuan jiakin.</li>

      <li>A suangphum tuh tang siangthoute ah a om hi.</li>

      <li>Pathian khopi aw, na tungtangthu thupi takin a gen uhi. Selah.</li>

      <li>A hi, hiai mi leh hua mi amaha piang ahi ua: Tungnungpen ngeiin amah tuh a hihkip ding, chih, Zion tungtangthu a gen ding uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN, mi chih min a gelh chiangin, Hiai mi tuh huaia piang ahi, chiin, a sim ding, Selah.Lasaten, a lamte toh, Ka tuikhuk tengteng tuh nangmah ah ahi a om, a chi ding uhi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA aw, honhumbitpa Pathian, sun leh janin na maah ka kikou gigea;</li>
      <li>Ka thumna na maah lut henla; ka kikou husa ah na bil hondohin;</li>
      <li>Ka hinna mangbatnatein a dima, ka hinnain Sheol a honnaihta ngala.</li>
      <li>Kokhuka paisukte laka sim khawm ka hi a; hatna himhim neilou mi bang ka hi a;</li>
      <li>Gal thahte han-a lumte banga misi laka paih khiak ka hi; huaite tuh na theih tak louh, na khut akipan hihman ahi uhi.</li>
      <li>Kokhuk nuainungpenah non lum sakta a, mun mial tak, thupi-ah.</li>
      <li>Na hehnain hondelh khuma, nang na tui kihawt tengtengin gim non thuaksakta a. Selah.</li>
      <li>Ka meltheihte hon gamlatin na om saka; amau adia kihhuai piin non bawlta a: khakkhumin ka oma, ka pawt khe theikei ahi.</li>
      <li>Gimthuakna jiakin ka mit a se hiaihiaia: TOUPA aw, ni tengin kon sam ahi, nang lamah ka khutte khawng ka jaka.</li>
      <li>Misite adingin thillamdang na hih dek ahia? Sisaten thouin a honphat ding ua hia? Selah.</li>
      <li>Na chitdan tuh hana theihsakin, na ginomdan tuh Manthatna Muna theihsakin a om dia hia?</li>
      <li>Na thillamdang hihte tuh mialah theihin a om dia hia? Na diktatna gamah theihin a om dek nawn ahia?</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, ken jaw kon sama, ka thumnain jingsangin a hondon hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA, bangachia ka hinna khah khia na hia? Bangachia ka laka na mai sel?</li>
      <li>Ka naupan chil akipan gimthuak leh si dekdekin ka oma; na thil mulkimhuaite ka thuakin hihlungbuaiin ka om hi:</li>
      <li>Na heh mahmahnain hon vuk manga; na thil mulkimhuaiten honhihmangta a.</li>
      <li>Huaiten nitumin tui bangin honumsuak ua; ka kim ka velin honum chiat uhi.Honitpa leh ka lawm tuh hon gamlatin a omsakta a, ka mel theihnate mial ah na omsakta ahi.</li>
      <li>Honitpa leh ka lawm tuh hon gamlatin a omsakta a, ka mel theihnate mial ah na omsakta ahi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA chitna thute tuh khantawnin lain ka sa dinga: ka kamin na ginomdan suan tengteng tanin ka theisak ding.</li>
      <li>Chitna tuh khantawn adingin leptouhin a om dinga; na ginomna tuh vante ah ngei na hihkip ding, ka chita ahi.</li>
      <li>Ka mitel kiangah thu ka khunga, ka sikha David kiangah ka kichiamta a;</li>
      <li>Na suante khantawn adingin ka hihkip dinga, na laltutphah leng suan tengteng taninka lemtou ding, chiin. Selah.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, vanten na thillamdang hih a phat ding uh; mi siangthoute kikhopna ah na ginomna leng a phat ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Tung vandumte ah TOUPA toh kiteh thei ding kua a oma? Mi thilhihhhteitak tate laka TOUPA bang.</li>
      <li>Mi siangthoute kihou khawmna ah Pathian kihtakhuai tak, a kim khawnga mi tengteng sanga kihtakpen ding, kua ahia?</li>
      <li>TOUPA sepaihte Pathian aw, A aw, nang banga mi hat kua a oma? Na ginomna na kimah a om ngala.</li>
      <li>Nang tuipi kisaktheihna vai na hawma: a tuikihawt kisep laite uh na hihdai hi.</li>
      <li>Nang Rahab gal thah bangin na hihkham dimdema; nangmah galte tuh na ban tha hatin na keksakta hi.</li>
      <li>Vante nangmaha ahi a, lei leng nangmaha ahi: khovel leh a sunga omteng nangmah muhkhiak ahi.</li>
      <li>Sim leh mal nangmah siam ahia: Tabor leh Hermon na min jiak in a nuam hi.</li>
      <li>Nang ban thilhihtheitak na neia: na khut a hata, na khut taklam tuh pahtawiin a om hi.</li>
      <li>Diktatna leh vaihawmna dik tuh na laltutphah kingakna ahi a: chitna leh thutak tuh n amaah a pai hi.</li>
      <li>Husa kipahhuai ja, namten nuam a sa ua: TOUPA aw, amau tuh na mel vakah a vak uhi.</li>
      <li>Na min jiakin nitumin a nuam ua, diktatna jiakin pahtawiin a om uhi.</li>
      <li>Nang ahatna uh thupina na ahi ngala: na deihsakna jiakin ka ki uh pahtawiin a om ding.</li>
      <li>Ka phaw uh TOUPA a ahi ngala: ka kumpipa uh Israelte Mi Siangthou ahi.</li>
      <li>Huai laiin na mi siangthoute kiangah kilaknain thu na gena, mi hattak khat tungah panpihna ka ngaa; mi khat mite laka tel khiak ka pahtawita hi, chiin.</li>
      <li>Ka sikha David tuh ka mukheta a; ka thau siangthouin amah ka nilhtaa:</li>
      <li>Ka khut a kiangah hihkipin a om dinga; ka banin amah a hihhat dinga; ka banin amah a hihat ding hi.</li>
      <li>Melmain a lakah a phut kei ding; thulimlouhna tain leng a hihgim kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Amah galte a maah ka sat puk dinga, amah hote ka bawl ek ding.</li>
      <li>Amah kiangah bel ka ginomna leh ka chitna a om ding hi; ka min jiakin a ki tuh pahtawiin a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>A khut tuh tuipi-ah ka nga sak dinga, a khut taklam tuh luipite ah.</li>
      <li>Aman, Nang ka Pa, ka Pathian, ka kihotdamna suangpi na hi, chiin, honsam ding.</li>
      <li>Huan, ken amah tuh ta masain ka siam dinga, leia kumpipate lakah tungnungpenin ka bawl ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka chitna tuh khantawnin amah adingin ka kep hoih sak dinga, ka thukhun tuh a kiangah a om kip ding hi.</li>
      <li>A chi suante tuh khantawnin ka omsak dinga, a laltutphah van om lai siahin ka omsak ding hi.</li>
      <li>A taten ka dan a lehngatsan ua, ka vaihawmnate banga a om louh ua.</li>
      <li>Ka thuseh a tatlekna a neih ua, ka thupiakte a kep hoih kei uleh.</li>
      <li>A tatleknate uh chiangin ka hongkan dinga, a thulimlouhnate uh jepin ka hongkan ding hi.</li>
      <li>Himahleh, ka chitna tuin a kiang akipan ka laksak vek kei dinga, ka ginomna tuh juau a suak din leng ka phal sam kei ding.</li>
      <li>Ka thukhun ka suse kei dinga, ka muka thupawt leng ka hihlamdang sam kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Khatvei ka siangthouna louin ka kichiama, David kiangah juau ka gen kei ding;</li>
      <li>A chi suante tuh khantawnin a om ding ua, a laltutphah ka maah ni bangin a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>Kha bangin khantawn adingin hihkipin a om dinga, van duma theihpih ginom bangin, a chi a, Selah.</li>
      <li>Himahleh nang na khahkhiain na deih keia, na thau nilhpa tungah na hehta ahi,</li>
      <li>Na sikha thukhun tuh na kiha: a lallukhu leia pai khe hialin na hihniamta hi.</li>
      <li>A huang tengteng na hihpuka; a kulh pite na hihse ta hi.</li>
      <li>Lampi a pai peuhmahin a thil a laksak jel uh.</li>
      <li>Amah doute khut taklam tuh na pahtawia; a melma tengteng na hihnuamsata hi,</li>
      <li>Ahi, a namsau ma tuh na beng peka, amah tuh kisualna ah na ding kip sakta kei hi.</li>
      <li>A vakna tuh na hihtawp saka, a laltutphah leiah na pai kheta hi.</li>
      <li>A tangvallai nite uh na hihtom saka; amah tuh zahlaknain na khuhta ngala. Selah.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, bangtan ahia na buk nilouh ding? Bangtan ahia na hehna tuh mei banga a kuan ding?</li>
      <li>Aw, ka hun a tom dingdan theigige inla; mihing tate tengteng siam gina kei natel chia!</li>
      <li>Kua mi ahia sih ni mel mulou ahinga, Sheol khut akipana a hinna humbit ding? Selah.</li>
      <li>TOUPA, nidanglaia na hehpihna, na ginomna David kianga kichiama na chiam, koia om a hita a?</li>
      <li>TOUPA, na sikhate a gensiatnauh theigige in; nam hat takte tengteng gensiatna ka angsunga ka thuak jeldan.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang hondoute gensiatna, na thaunilhpa khapte gensiatna mah,TOUPA tuh khantawnin phatin om hen. Amen, Amen.</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh khantawnin phatin om hen. Amen, Amen.</li>
    </ol>

      <li>TOUPA, nang tuh suan tengteng tana ka omna uh na hia.</li>

      <li>Nang mihing tuh manthatna ah na kiksaka; Mihingtate aw, kik un, na chi jel hi.</li>
      <li>Nang sehin kum sang khat tuh janmangta bang phet ahi ngala, jan ven khat sung bang phet ahi.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh tui lian bangin na taimang a; khang khat ihmu bang phet ahi uh: jingsanga loupa dawn khia bang ahi uh.</li>
      <li>Jingsangin a hongpouin a hongdawn khiaa; nitaklamin phukin a oma, a vuai hi.</li>
      <li>Na hehna a hihmanin ka om ua, na thangpaihna a hihmangbata leng ka om jiak un.</li>
      <li>Ka thulimlouhnate uh na maah na koiha, ka khelhna gukte uh na mel vakah na koihta hi.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung ni tengteng uh na hehna ah a mang jela: ka dam sung kumte uh tangthu bangin ka tawpsak uhi.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung kumte uh kum sawmsagih a hi-a, hatna jiakin kum sawmgiat leng ahi thei hi; himahleh a sawtna tuh sepgimna leh lungngaihna lel a hi-a; a mang paha, kou leng ka leng mang jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Kuan ahia na hehna thilhihtheihdan theia, nangmah kihtak dingdan banga na hehna theilou?</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Chitna leh vaihawmna dik thu tuh lain ka sa dinga: TOUPA aw, nangmah phatin la ka sa ding..</li>
      <li>Lam hoih kimah pil takin ka om dinga: aw chikchiangin ahia ka kianga na hongpai ding? Ka in sungah lungtang hoihkim puin ka om ding hi.</li>
      <li>Thil hoihlou himhim ka mitmuhah ka koih kei ding: lam pialte thilhih ka hua ahi; keimah ah bang kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Lungtang genhakin honpaisan dinga: thil gilou himhim ka theikei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Kuapeuh a vengte a guka gen tuh, huai mi tuh ka hihmang dinga: mi sang leh lungtang kisathei pu mi tuh ka thuak theikei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Hiai gama mi muanhuaite tungah ka mit a tu dinga, ka kianga a om theihna ding un: lam hoihkim tawn tuh, huai miin ka na a sem ding hi.</li>
      <li>Khemhat tuh ka in sungah a omkei dinga: juauhat mi tuh ka mitmuhah hihkipin a om kei ding hi.Jingsang tengin hiai gama mi gilousalou tengteng ka hihmang dinga: TOUPA khopi akipan thilhihkhialte tengteng hihmang dingin.</li>
      <li>Jingsang tengin hiai gama mi gilousalou tengteng ka hihmang dinga: TOUPA khopi akipan thilhihkhialte tengteng hihmang dingin.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA aw, ka thumna ngaikhia inla, ka kikou husa na kiang tung hen.</li>
      <li>Ka mangbat niin ka lakah na mai sel kenla: kei lamah na bil hondohin; ka honsap hun chiangin hondawng pahin.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung nite meikhu bangin a jam manga, ka guhte tuh taptung bangin a saa.</li>
      <li>Ka lungtang tuh loupa bangin hailumin a oma, a vuai zouta hi; ann nek leng ka mangngilhta ngala.</li>
      <li>Ka thum husa jiakin ka guhte tuh ka sa ah a belh bikbek ahi.</li>
      <li>Gamdai tuivapi bang ka hi a: kho tul simbu bang phet ka na hita hi.</li>
      <li>Ka hak gige a, kawlgit in tunga amah kiaa om bang ka na hita hi.</li>
      <li>Hondouten nitumin hon gensia ua: ka tunga hangsanten keimah banga om dingin hamsia a lou nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Vut tuh an bangin ka ne a, ka dawn dingin khitui toh ka helta ngala.</li>
      <li>Na lunghih louh mahmah leh na heh jiakin: nang non dom kanga, na honpai mangta ngala.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung nite tuh limliap kiam bang ahi a; loupa bangin ka vuaita hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang bel khantawnin na om dinga; nangmah theihgigena leng suan tengteng phain a om lai ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na thou dinga, Zion tang tuh na hehpih dinga: amah lah hehpih a hunta ngala, ahi, hun seh tuh a tungta hi.</li>
      <li>Na sikhaten a suangte a it un, a leivui leng a hehpih ngal uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchiin nam chihin TOUPA mintuh a lau ding ua, leia kumpipate tengtengin na thupina leng a lau ding uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN Zion khua dingsakta ngala, a thupina kithuamin a kimuta hi;</li>
      <li>Tagahte thumna tuh a limsaka, a thumna uh a musit kei hi.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh khangthak hongom ding adingin gelh ahi dinga: nam siama hongom di in TOUPA tuh a phat ding.</li>
      <li>Aman a mun siangthou sangpi akipanin a en suka; TOUPAN van akipanin lei a mu a;</li>
      <li>Suangkulhtang thum ngaikhe ding leh, si dinga sehte sut dingin;</li>
      <li>Huchi-a miten Ziona TOUPA min tuh a genthang ua, Jerusalema a phatna tuh a genthang theihna ding un.</li>
      <li>Mite a kikhawm khawm ua, lalgamte toh, TOUPA nasem ding in.</li>
      <li>Aman lam lakah ka tha a bahsaka; ka damsung tuh a hihtom hi.</li>
      <li>Ka Pathian aw, ka hatlai nite khawngin honla mang ken, ka chia: nang kum tuh suan om sung tengtengin a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>Leitung kingakna tuh nidanga na phum sa ahi a; vante leng na khutsuak ahi.</li>
      <li>Huaite tuh a hongmang dinga, nangjaw na om tawntung ding hi: ahi, huai tengteng tuh puansilh bangin a honglui dinga; puan bangin na khek dinga, a honglamdangta ding hi.</li>
      <li>Nang jaw na ngeingeia, na kumten bei ni himhim a neikei ding.Na sikhate tate tuh a om gige ding ua, a suangte uh na maah hihkipin a om ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Na sikhate tate tuh a om gige ding ua, a suangte uh na maah hihkipin a om ding uhi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ka hinna aw, TOUPA phat inla; ka sunga om tengteng aw, a min siangthou phat in!</li>
      <li>Ka hinna aw, TOUPA phat inla, a thilhih hoih tengteng mangngilh ken.</li>
      <li>Aman na thulimlouhna tengteng a ngaidam jela; na natna tengteng a hihdam jel.</li>
      <li>Manthatna lak akipan nahinna a tan jela; chitna leh lainatnate a honkhusak jel hi.</li>
      <li>Na kam tuh thil hoihin a taisaka; huchiin na valnouna mupi banga siam thakin a om nawn naknak hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN, nuaisiaha thuak tengteng adingin, thil kizente hihsakin, vaite a hawmsak nak hi.</li>
      <li>A lampite Mosi a theisaka, a thilhihte tuh Israel suante leng a theisak hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh lainatnaa dim, mi hehpihtheitak, lungnel tak, chitna hautak ahi.</li>
      <li>Aman a taikei dinga; a hehna tuh a pai nilouhlouh sam kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>I khelhnate bangin I tunguah a hih keia, I thulimlouhnate bangin leng a honthuk sam kei hi.</li>
      <li>Van leitung sang taka a om bangin, amah laute tungah a chitna tuh a lian mahmah ahi.</li>
      <li>Suahlam leh tumlama kigamlat bangin, I tatlekna te tuh eimah a kipan in a koih mgangta hi.</li>
      <li>Pa in a tate a hehpih bangin, TOUPAN amah laute tuh a hehpih naknak.</li>
      <li>I pumpi kibawldan a theia, leivui lel I hi chih a theih jiakin.</li>
      <li>Mihing jaw, a damsung nite loupa bang ahi a; pawna pak bangin a lun nak hi.</li>
      <li>Huihin a muta, a mang jel ahi; a omnain a thei nawnta kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA chitna bel amah kihtate tungah khantawn akipanin khantawn phain a om dinga, a diktatna leng a tusuan a tasuan tan un a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>A thukhun jui peuhmahte leh, a thuhilhte man tuma theigige peuhmahte tungah.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN a laltutphah tuh vanah a hihkipa; a gamin bangkim tungah vai a hawm hi.</li>
      <li>A thu ngaikhia a, a thumang nou a angelten aw, hatnaa thupite aw, TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>
      <li>A sepaihte aw, a deihlam hiha nasemte aw, TOUPA tuh phat un.A vaihawmna mun peuhmaha a thilhih tengteng aw, TOUPA tuh phat un: ka hinna aw, TOUPA tuh phatin.</li>
      <li>A vaihawmna mun peuhmaha a thilhih tengteng aw, TOUPA tuh phat un: ka hinna aw, TOUPA tuh phatin.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ka hinna aw, TOUPA tuh phatin, TOUPA ka Pathian aw, nang na thupi mahmaha; pahtawinain leh thupinain na kithuam hi.</li>
      <li>Nang vak tuh puan bangin na silha; vante puanintung bangin na kai palha;</li>
      <li>Aman a dantan sunggil kalvaite tuite khawngah a khunga; meipi tuh kangtalaiin a bawla; huih kha tungah a vak hi:</li>
      <li>A angelten tuh huihina suaksaka; a nasemte tuh meikuang juajuain a suaksak hi.</li>
      <li>Leitung kingaknate tuh na phuma, khantawna lin louhna dingin.</li>
      <li>Nang leilung tuh thukpi puan bangin na silhsaka; tuite tang tungah tekhawng a om pheuphou hi.</li>
      <li>Na taihilhna jiakin a taimanga; na van-ging husa jiakina paimang pahta a;</li>
      <li>Tang khawngah a pai tou a, guam ah tekhawng a pai suka, amah dia mun na bawlsakna lamah.</li>
      <li>A kan louh dingin gi na khunga, lei tup mang dinga a kiknawn tak louhna dingin.</li>
      <li>Aman guam ahte khawng luinakte a sawl khiaa; tangkal khawngah a luang hi.</li>
      <li>Huaiten tuh gamsa khempeuh kiangah dawnding a pia ua; Gam sabengtungten a dangtak uh a hihdai uhi.</li>
      <li>A dung uah tungleng vasaten omna a nei ua, singbawk lak khawngah a ham uhi.</li>
      <li>Aman a dantan tungnung akipanin tangte tuiin a vaka: lei tuh na thilhih gahtein a vaka: lei tuh na thilhih gahtein a tai uhi.</li>
      <li>Loupa gante adingin a pousaka, haichi tuh mihing zatdin a pousak hi: lei akipan nekding pawtsak theihna dingin:</li>
      <li>Mihing lungtang kipahsakna uain toh, a mai kilawmsakna ding thau toh, mihing lungtang hihhatna tanghou toh.</li>
      <li>TOUPA singte tuh a taisak hi; Lebanon tanga sidar sing a suante mah.</li>
      <li>Huaiah vasaten bu a sep ua: vaiva bel meilah singte a in ahi.</li>
      <li>Tang sangte sathak ading ahi a; suangpite zusapi adingin kihumbitna ahi.</li>
      <li>Aman kha hunbi theihna dingin a sepa: niin tum hun theigige hi.</li>
      <li>Nang mial na bawla, jan a honghi jel hi, huai hunin gamnuaia sa khempeuhte a ta khia uhi.</li>
      <li>Humpinelkai hatlaiten a sa mat ding uh, humham khumin, Pathian kiang akipan a nekding uh a zong uhi.</li>
      <li>Ni suaka, a pai mang uh, a omna khuk chiat uah a lum jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Mihing tuh na semin apawta, nitaklam tanin a semgim hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na thilhihte tam hina tele! Pilnain na bawl vek ahi; leilung na hauhsaknain a dim hi.</li>
      <li>Pamah tuipi a oma, thupi, lianpi tak, huaiah thil bokvaka pai sim zohlouh a oma, sa neu leh sa liante.</li>
      <li>Huailaiah meilong liante a pai uh; huailaiah ole a om, a sunga mawl dinga na bawl ngei.</li>
      <li>Huai tengtengin a honngak chiat ua, a huntaka a ann uh na piak jelna dingin.</li>
      <li>A kiang ua na piak peuhmah a tawm ua; na khut ua jaka, hoihnain a tai jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Na mai na sela, a lungjing ua, a hatna uh na laksaka, a si ua, amau leivui ah a kik nawn uhi.</li>
      <li>Na kha na sawl khiaa, siamin a om jel uhi; leitung leng na bawl thak nawn jel hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA thupina tuh khantawin om henla; TOUPA tuh a nasepah nuam hen:</li>
      <li>Aman lei a ena, a ling nak; tangte a khoiha, a khu khe nak hi.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung tengin TOUPA pahtawiin la ka sa dinga: ka hinlai tengin ka Pathian phatin la ka sa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka ngaihtuahna tuh amaha dingin khumtak hi hen: kei tuh TOUPA ah ka nuam ding hi.Mi khialte lei akipanin hihmanin om uhenla, mi gilou-saloute om nawnta kei uhen! Ka hinna aw, TOUPA phatin! TOUPA tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>Mi khialte lei akipanin hihmanin om uhenla, mi gilou-saloute om nawnta kei uhen! Ka hinna aw, TOUPA phatin! TOUPA tuh phat un!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Aw, TOUPA kiangah kipahthu gen unla, amin lou un; mi chih lakah a thilhihte theisak un.</li>
      <li>Amah pahtawiin lasa unla, amah phatin lasa un; a thillamdang hih tengteng thuin houlim un.</li>
      <li>A min siangthou tuh suang un: TOUPA zongte lungtang nuamsa hen.</li>
      <li>TOUPA leh a hatna zong unla: a mel zong gige un.</li>
      <li>A hihzohsa a nasep lamdangte, a thillamdangte, leh a kama vaihawmnate tuh theigige un;</li>
      <li>A sikha Abraham suante aw, a telte Jakob tate aw.</li>
      <li>Amah tuh TOUPA i Pathian ahi a; a vaihawmte leitung tengtengah a om hi.</li>
      <li>A thukhun khantawnin a thei naknak, suan sang khat tana a thu na piak ngei;</li>
      <li>Abraham kianga a thukhun leh, Isaak kianga a kichiamna ngei;</li>
      <li>Huaimah tuh thuseh adingin Jakob kiangah a hihkipa, Israel kiang khantawn thukhun dingin.</li>
      <li>Kanaan gam na kiangah ka honpe dinga, na gou tantuam ding chiin.</li>
      <li>Mi tawmchik phet a hihlai un; ahi, tawmchik phet, huai gamah mikhual ahi ngal ua;</li>
      <li>Nam tuamtuam kiangah a pai vialvial ua, gam tuamtuam akipanin mi tuamtuamte kiangah.</li>
      <li>Kuamah nuaisiah a phal keia: ahi, amau jiakin kumpipate leng a taihilha:</li>
      <li>Ka thaunilhte khoih kei unla, ka jawlneite himhim leng hihna kei un, chiin.</li>
      <li>Huai gama ke dingin kial a sam a; nek ding himhim a omsakta kei hi.</li>
      <li>A ma uah mi a sawla; Joseph sikha dinga juakin a oma:</li>
      <li>A khete tuh kolin a hihna ua; sik khainiang bunin a omta a.</li>
      <li>A thu a tun masiah, TOUPA thuin amah tuh a zeet ngitnget hi.</li>
      <li>Kumpipan mi a sawl khiaa, a suta, a khahta a, mi chih vaihawmpa ngeiin.</li>
      <li>A innsunga heutu ding leh, a sum tengteng tunga vaihawm dingin a bawla:</li>
      <li>A mi liante a ututa hen ding leh; a upate hihpil dingin.</li>
      <li>Israel leng Aigupta gamah a hoha; Jakob tuh Ham gamah a omta dih hi.</li>
      <li>A mite tuh nakpi takin a pungsaka, amau doute sangin a hihhat zota hi.</li>
      <li>A mite ho dingin a lungtang uh a lehngatsaka, a sikhate tunga lepchiah taka hih dingin.</li>
      <li>A sikha Mosi a sawla, a mitel Aron toh.</li>
      <li>Amau achiamnate a lak uah a ensak ua, Ham gamah thillamdangte a ensak uhi.</li>
      <li>Aman mial a sawla, a hihmialta a; huchiin a thute tuh a nialta kei uhi.</li>
      <li>A tuite uh sisan a suaksaka, a ngasate uh a hihlumta hi.</li>
      <li>A gam uh ukengin a dimta a, a kumpipate uh dantan sungah nangawn leng.</li>
      <li>Aman thu a gena, huchiin thou tampi hongpai ua, hik leng a gamsung tengteng uah a hongom uhi.</li>
      <li>A kiang uah vuah sikin gial a pia a, a gam uah meikuang jualjual leng a peta hi.</li>
      <li>A grep guite u leh a theipi kungte uh a hihsi a; a gam ua singte leng a kitansakta hi.</li>
      <li>Aman thu a gena, huchiin khaupeta a hongpai ua, lungte toh, sim zoh vuallouhin.</li>
      <li>Huaiten a gam ua haichi khempeuh a gai ua, a lei gahte uleng a gai uhi.</li>
      <li>A gam ua ta masa om tengteng a thata, a hatna tengteng gah masapente uh.</li>
      <li>Huchiin, dangka leh dangkaeng toh a pi kheta a; amah namte lakah mi hatlou khat leng a om kei hi.</li>
      <li>A pawt lai un Aiguptate a kipak ua: amau tuh a lau tak jiak un.</li>
      <li>Aman aliah dingin mei a kaisaka, jana tanvak dingin mei leng a pia hi.</li>
      <li>A ngen ua, huchiin vamin a honpia a, van an-in amau a taisakta hi,</li>
      <li>Suangpi a honga, huchiin tui a hongpawt juajua a, mun keute ah lui bangmaiin a luangta hi.</li>
      <li>A thu siangthou a theigige ngala, a sikha Abraham toh.</li>
      <li>Huchiin, a mite tuh nuamsa takin a pi kheta a, a mitelte tuh lasa kawmkawm jelin.</li>
      <li>Huan, nam chih gamte a kiang uah a piaksaka: amau tuh mi chih sepkhiaksa a luahta uhi.A thusehte a zuih theihna ding un, a dante tuh a vom hoihna dingin, TOUPA phat un.</li>
      <li>A thusehte a zuih theihna ding un, a dante tuh a vom hoihna dingin, TOUPA phat un.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA tuh phat un, Aw, TOUPA kiangah kipahthu hilh un; amah lah a hoih ngala: a chitna leng khantawna om ding ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Kua ahia TOUPA thilhih thupitakte gen theia a phatna tengteng theisak vek thei?</li>
      <li>Vaihawmna kem hoihten nuam a sa uhi, chiklai peuha leng diktat taka hihmi toh.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na mite na deihsaknain hontheigige inla, aw, na hotdamna toh hongvehin;</li>
      <li>Na mi telte hamphatna ka muhtheiha, na namte kipahna ah ka nopsak theiha, na gouluahte toh ka suan theihna dingin.</li>
      <li>Ka pipute utoh thil ka na hihkhial ua, thilgilou ka hih ua, gilou takinka hihta uhi.</li>
      <li>Ka pipute un Aigupta gama na thillamdang hihte a theisiam kei ua; na chitna thupitak a theigige ta kei ua; tuipi ah a hel zota ua, Tuipi San ah.</li>
      <li>Huchi pipiin leng a mah minjiakin amau a hondamtaa, a thilhihtheihna thupitak a theihsakna dingin.</li>
      <li>Tuipi San a taia, huchiin a kangta a; huan amau gamdaia pi paisuak bangin tui thukte ah a pi paisuakta hi.</li>
      <li>Amau homi khut akipan a hondama, melma khut akipan a tanta hi.</li>
      <li>Tuiten amau doute a khuh khina, khat leng dama pawt a om ta kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Huai laiin a thute a gingta ua; a phatna la a sa uhi.</li>
      <li>Himahleh a thilhihte tuh a mangngilh zok ua; a lunggelna tuh a ngak ngamta kei uhi;</li>
      <li>Gamdai ah thil a lungulh mahmah ua, gam keu ah Pathian a zeetta uhi.</li>
      <li>A thil nget uh a pia a; himahleh a hinna uah gawnna a lutsakta hi.</li>
      <li>A giah mun uah Mosi a hazata ua, TOUPA mi siangthou Aron toh.</li>
      <li>Lei tuh a kamkaa, Dathan a valhta, Abiram pawlte tuh a khuh khinvek hi.</li>
      <li>A pawl lak uah mei hihkuanin a hongoma, meikuang ah mi gilousaloute a kangmangta uhi.</li>
      <li>Horeb tang ah bawngnou lim a siam ua, a lim sun tuh a beta uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchibangin a thupina uh bawngtal loupa ne bangphet a suaksakta uhi.</li>
      <li>Pathian a hondampa uh a mangngilhta ua, Aigupta gama thil thupi taktak.</li>
      <li>Ham gama thillamdangte, Tuipi San dung athil mulkimhuaite hihte.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin, a hihmang kha dinga, chi-a, a hehna hihkik dingin a mi tel Mosi tuh a lutna dingah a maah na ding kei ngial le houh, a hihmang ding chih a gen hi.</li>
      <li>A hi, gam deihhuai tak a ngaineu ua, a thu tuh a gingta nuam kei ua;</li>
      <li>A puanin uahte khawng a phun zota ua, TOUPA aw tuh a ngaikhe nuam kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin amau lamah a khut ajaka, amaute tuh gamdaia a hihpukna ding leh,</li>
      <li>A chi suan dingte uh nam chih laka a hihpuka, gam china a hihjakna dingin.</li>
      <li>Boal-peor lamah a velh ua, misi kianga thil latte tuh a ne samta uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchibangin a thilhihte un amah a hihheh ua; huchiin a tunguah hi honlengta hi.</li>
      <li>Huai laiin Phinehas a dinga, vai a hawma: huchiin hi tuh daihsakin a omta hi.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh amah tunga diktatnaa seh ahi, khantawnin suan tengteng tanin.</li>
      <li>Meribah tuite ah tekhawng leng amah a hihheh ua, huchiin amau jiakin Mosi tungah thilhoihlou a tung hialta hi.</li>
      <li>A kha tungah a hel ua, a mukin kilawmlou pi thu a gen jiakin;</li>
      <li>TOUPAN a kiang ua hihman thu a piak bangin mipite a hihmang kei ua.</li>
      <li>Nam chih tuh a kihelpih ua, a thilhihte uh tuh a ching jaw ua;</li>
      <li>A milim nate khawng uh a sem ua; huaite tuh amau adingin thang a honghita:</li>
      <li>A hi, dawi kiangah tekhawng a tapate a tanute un a kithoih ua.</li>
      <li>Sisan gensiatbei, a tapate uleh a tanute u sisan ngei a suahta ua, huaitein Kanaan gam milimte kiangah a kithoih uhi; huai gam tuh sisanin a na ninta hi.</li>
      <li>Huchibangin a nasepte ua hihbuahin a om ua, a thilhihte un ang a kawmta uhi.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin TOUPA a mit tungah a thangpaitaa, a gouluah tuh a kih hi.</li>
      <li>Huchiin amau tuh nam chihkhut ah a paia; amau hoten a tunguah vai a hawmta uhi.</li>
      <li>Amau douten a nuaisiah ua, a khut nuai uah hihneuin a omta uhi.</li>
      <li>Tamveipi amau a humbita; himahleh a lunggelna uah a hel nak uhi, a gitlou a satlouhna uah hihniamin aomta uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchi pipiin leng aman, a kikou husa uh a jain, a mangbat uh a limsak ahi.</li>
      <li>A thukhun tuh amau a theisak gigea a chitna thupidan bang jelin alungsim a kisikta hi.</li>
      <li>Sala pite tengteng tuh amau a hehpihsak hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA ka Pathian u-aw, honhondam inla, nam chih laka kipan honpikhawmin, na min siangthou phat ding leh na phatna suang dingin.TOUPA, Israelte Pathian, phatin om heh, khantawn akipan khantawn phain leng. Mi tengtengin, Amen, chi uhen, TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>
      <li>TOUPA, Israelte Pathian, phatin om heh, khantawn akipan khantawn phain leng. Mi tengtengin, Amen, chi uhen, TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Aw TOUPA kiangah kipahthu hilh un; amah tuh a hoih ngala: a chitna leng khantawnin a om ding ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>TOUPA mi tatten huchibang gen uhen, doumi khut akipan a tatten.</li>
      <li>Gam teng akipan a pi khawma, suahlam leh tumlam, simlam leh mallam akipan tekhawngin.</li>
      <li>Gamdaia gam keu lampi ah a vakvak ua; mihing omna khua himhim a mu kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Gilkial leh dangtakin a hinna uh a gilsung uah a bahta hi.</li>
      <li>Huaitakin a buaina uah TOUPA a sam ua, aman a lungkhamna ua kipanin a humbitta.</li>
      <li>Mihing omna khuaa a pai theihna ding un, lampi tangtak ah a pikheta hi.</li>
      <li>Aw, mihingten TOUPA a chitna jiak leh, mihing tate tunga a thillamdang hihte jiakin phat himhim le u aw!</li>
      <li>Aman hinna thil lunggulh mahmah tuh a taisakin, hinna gilkial tuh vahsak jel ngala.</li>
      <li>Mial nuaia leh sihna lima tu-a, gimthuakna leh sikkhau a hente mahmah;</li>
      <li>Pathian thu tungahte a hel ua, Tungnungpen lunggel tuh a ngaihneu jiak un:</li>
      <li>Aman a lungtang uh sepgimnain a minsakta a; a puk ua, panpihpa ding himhim lah a om ngal kei a.</li>
      <li>Huai takin a buaina uah TOUPA a sam ua, aman a buaina ua kipan a pi khia a, a hennate uh a suktat sakta hi.</li>
      <li>Mial nuai akipan leh sihna lim akipan a pi khia a, a henna uh a suktat sakta hi.</li>
      <li>Aw, mihingten TOUPA a chitna jiakin leh, mihing tate tunga a thillamdang hihte jiakin phat himhim le u aw!</li>
      <li>Aman dal kongkhakte tuh a chimsaka, a kalhna sik tawnte tuh a hihtanta ngala.</li>
      <li>Mi haite a tatlekna jiak un leh, a gitlouh-satlouhnate u jiakin a kihihgim nak uhi.</li>
      <li>A hinna un nek theih chiteng a kiha; sihna kulh kongkhakte a naih jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Huaitakin a buaina uah TOUPA a sam ua, aman a mangbatna ua kipanin a hondam jel hi.</li>
      <li>A thu tuh a sawl khia a, amau tuh a damsak jel hi, a mahthatna ding ua kipanin a humbit jel hi.</li>
      <li>Aw, mihingten TOUPA a chitna jiakin leh, mihing tate tunga a thillamdang hihte jiakinphat himhim leu aw!</li>
      <li>Amau kipahthugen kithoihnate tuh lan uhenla, a thilhihte uh lasain hilh uhen.</li>
      <li>Tuipi-a long liana vapai suka, tui za tak tung khawnga na sem semten:</li>
      <li>Huaiten TOUPA thilhihte leh, tui thupi-a a thillamdang hihte a mu jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Aman thu a pia a, huihpi a nungsaka, huaiin a tuikihawtte tuh a sangsak hi.</li>
      <li>Vanah a pai tou luamluam ua, thukpi ah a pai suk nawn luamluam jel uhi: mangbatna jiakin a hinna uh a zulbei jel hi.</li>
      <li>Zukham bangin a sawi hoihoi ua, a tuan loklok ua, omdan ding himhim a theikei nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Huaitakin a buaina uah TOUPA a sam ua, aman a mangbatna ua kipanin a pi jel hi.</li>
      <li>Huihpi a daisak duama, huchiin a tuikihawtte a dai duam jel hi.</li>
      <li>Huan, a daihtak jiakin a kipak ua; huchiin aman a omna ding uh longkhawlna ah a pi tung jel hi.</li>
      <li>Aw, mihingten TOUPA a chitna jiakin leh, mihing tate tunga a thillamdang hihte jiakin phat mahmah le u-aw!</li>
      <li>Amau tuh mite kikhopna ah amah phat uhenla, upate tutana ah phat uhen.</li>
      <li>Aman luipite tuh gamdai a suaksak jela, tuinakte leng lei keu a suaksak jel hi.</li>
      <li>Gam hoih tuh gam keu mah leng a suaksak jel, a sunga omte genhak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Gamdai tuh dilin a suaksak jela, gam keu leng tuinak a suaksak jel hi.</li>
      <li>Huaiah gilkialte a omsaka, omna ding khua a bawl ua.</li>
      <li>Loute a neih ua, grep huante a bawl ua, a gah hong pungte a muh theihna ding un.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh vual a jawla, huchiin nakpi taka hihpunin a om ua; a gante uh a kiam a phal kei hi.</li>
      <li>Huan, nuaisiahte, gimthuaknate, lungkhamna te jiakin a kiamta hiaihiai ua, a kun ngiungiauta leuleu uhi.</li>
      <li>Aman miliante tungah muhsitna a sungbuaa, gamdai, lampi himhim omlouhna ah a vak saksaka.</li>
      <li>Himahleh gentheite tuh gimthuakna akipanin mun sangah a khatou hi, gan hon bangin inkuanpihte asiamsak hi.</li>
      <li>Mi diktatten huai a mu ding ua, a kipak ding uh; thulimlouhna tengtengin a kam a hum ding hi.Kuapeuh pilin huaite a kem hoih ding ua, TOUPA chitnate a ngaihtuah ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Kuapeuh pilin huaite a kem hoih ding ua, TOUPA chitnate a ngaihtuah ding uhi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Pathian aw, ka lungtang a kip hi; la a sa ding, ahi, phatna la ka sa ding, ka thupina ngeiin.</li>
      <li>Pekging leh kaihging te aw, halh un: kei jaw jingkhangin ka halh ding.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, mi chih lakah tekhawng kipahthu ka honhilh ding: nam chih lakah nangmah phatin la kasa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na chitna tuh van khup hialin a thupi ngala, na thutakin vandumte leng a sun hial hi.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, nang van khup thamin pahtawiin hongom in: na thupina leitung tengteng tungah pahtawiin leng om hen.</li>
      <li>Na deih takte humbita a omtheihna ding un, na khut taklaminhondam inla, hondawngin.</li>
      <li>Pathianin a sianthouna ah hichibangin agena, Nuam ka sa dinga: Sekemkhua tuh ka hawm dinga, Sukkoth guam tuh ka hawmjak ding.</li>
      <li>Gilead gam tuh keia ahi a; Manasi gam leng ka lu humbitna ahi a: Juda gam tuh ka lalchiang ahi.</li>
      <li>Moab gam tuh ka kisilna bel ahia; Edom gamah ka khedap ka pai dinga; Philistia gam tuh ka kikou khum ding hi.</li>
      <li>Khopi kulhnei ah kuan a honpi lut dia? Edom gamah kuan a honpi dia?</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, nang honkhah khia hilou na hi maw? Pathian aw, ka sepaihhonte u kiangah lah na pawt samta ngal keia.</li>
      <li>Galte sual dingin honpanpihin: mihing panpihna jaw bangmahlou phet ahi ngala.Pathian jiakin hangtakin ka hih ding uh: amah lah hondoute sikdenpa ding ahi ngal.</li>
      <li>Pathian jiakin hangtakin ka hih ding uh: amah lah hondoute sikdenpa ding ahi ngal.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ka phat Pathian aw, dai nilouh ken:</li>
      <li>Migilou-salou kam leh kam khemhat tuh ka tungah a hang ngal ua: amau tuh lei juautheiin ka kiangah thu a gen uhi.</li>
      <li>Huatna thuin honum suak ua, bangmahlouin a hondou uhi.</li>
      <li>Ka it jiakin a hondoute a honghita uhi: himahleh kei jaw thum thum dingin ka kipe chinten hi.</li>
      <li>Aman thil hoih tuh thil gilouin honthuk ua, ka itna tuh huatna mahin a honthuk uhi.</li>
      <li>Nang a tungah mi gilou koih inla: a tak lamah hekmi ding hen.</li>
      <li>Vaihawmsaka a om chiangin siamlouh tangin pawt henla: a thumna tuh khelhna ah suak hen.</li>
      <li>A damsung nite tuh tom henla; a heutu hihna midangin tang hen.</li>
      <li>A tate tuh pa louin om uhenla, a ji mahleng meithaiin om hen.</li>
      <li>A tate tuh mi vakvai honghiin, khutdoh uhenla; a nekding uh a mun gamsiate ah zong uhen.</li>
      <li>A pung delha dangka leitawisakin a neih tengteng laksak vek henla; mikhualten a sepgim gah lok uhen.</li>
      <li>A tunga chitna langsak jel ding kuamah om sam kei uhenla; a ta paneiloute hehpihpa ding kuamah om kei hen.</li>
      <li>A suante hihmanin om uhen la; khangthak hongom nawnah a min uh nul mangin om hen.</li>
      <li>A pipute uh gitlouh-satlouhna TOUPA kiangah theigigein om henla: a nu khelhna tuh nul mangin om kei hen.</li>
      <li>Huaite tuh TOUPA maah om gige heh. Aman a mau theihgigena lei akipan a hihmang theihna dingin.</li>
      <li>Chitna latsak nadan a theihlouh ua, mi genthei tagah leh khasiate hihlup tuma a sawi zosop jiak un:</li>
      <li>A hi, mi hamsiat tuh a utlam ahi a, huchiin amah tungah a hongtunga: mi vualjawl tuh a kipahlam ahi keia, huchiin amah gamlat piin a om hi.</li>
      <li>Puanak tual silh bangin hamsiatnain a kivana, huai tuh a gilsung khawngah tui bangina luta, a guh khawngah thau bangin a leng lut hi.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh amah a dingin silh gige puansilh bangin om henla, a kigak jelna kawnggak mahleng hi hen.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh hondoute leh ka hinna gensete TOUPAN a thukna ahi.</li>
      <li>Himahleh, TOUPA Pathian aw, nang na min jiakin honhehpih inla: na chitna a hoih jiakin honhumbit in.</li>
      <li>Genthei leh tagah tak ka hia, ka lungtang tuh ka gilsungah liamin a om ngal hi.</li>
      <li>Lim kiamlam bangin ka manga: khaupe bangin mutlengin ka om hi.</li>
      <li>Ka khukte ann ngawl jiakin a hatta keia; ka sain thau himhim a puta kei hi.</li>
      <li>Amau gensiat ka nahita a; honmuh tak un a lu uh a sing jel uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA ka Pathian aw, honpanpih inla; aw na chitna bang jelin honhondamin;</li>
      <li>Huai tuh na khut ahi, chih a theih ua, TOUPA, nang na hih ahi chih a theihna ding un.</li>
      <li>Amau hamsiat uhen, nang jaw vualjawl jawin: a thoh tak un a zahlak ding ua, na sikha bel a nuamsa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Hondoute zumna puansilh sakin om uhenla, puannak-a kivan bangin amau zahlaknain kivan uhen.</li>
      <li>Ka kamin TOUPA kiangah kipahthu nakpi takin ka gen dinga; ahi, mipi lakah amah ka phat ding hi.Amah tuh tagahte taklamah a dinga, a hinna vaihawmsakte laka hondam dingin.</li>
      <li>Amah tuh tagahte taklamah a dinga, a hinna vaihawmsakte laka hondam dingin.</li>

    <ol>
      <li>TOUPAN, ka toupa kiangah, Na melmate na khe ngaknaa ka siam masiah ka taklamah tuin, a chi a.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN na hatna chiang Zion tang akipanin a sawlkhe ding: nang nangmah doute lakah vaihawmin.</li>
      <li>Na mite na thilhihtheihna ni-ah amau utthuin a kipe jel uhi. Siangthou kilawmna ah, jingsang gilsung akipanin, na valnou daitui tuh na nei hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA a kichiama, a kisik nawnta kei ding, Nang jaw Melkisedek omdan banga khantawn Siampu na hi a, chiin.</li>

      <li>Nam chih lakah vai a hawm dinga, munte tuh luang-in a hihdim dinga, gam tampi-ah lu tuh a sat kham lemlum ding hi.Lam laka luita a dawn dinga: huaijiakin a lu tuh a tawisang ding hi.</li>

      <li>TOUPA thilhihte tuh a thupi-a, a tunga kipak peuhten zon khiak ahi naknak hi.</li>
      <li>A nasep tuh a zahtakhuaiin a thupi ahi a; a diktatna tuh khantawna om ding ahi.</li>

      <li>Amah laute kiangah nekding a piaa; a thukhun tuh khawntawnin a theigige ding.</li>
      <li>A thilhihte thilhihtheihdan a mite kiangah a langsaka, nam chih gouluah ding a kiang ua piain.</li>

      <li>Huaite tuh khantawn khantawn adingin hihkipin a oma, thutak leh diktata hih ahi chiata.</li>

      <li>TOUPA tuh phat un, TOUPA kihta miin nuam a sa hi, a thupiaktea nakpi taka kipak miin.</li>

      <li>Mi hehpiha leitawisak jel mi tuh hoihin a vuk naka; amah tuh kizen takin a khosa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Bangchikmah chianga ling lou ding ahi ngala: mi diktat tuh khawntawna theihgigein a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>Tanchin hoihlou takte a lau kei ding: TOUPA muangin a lungtang tuh a kip ahi.</li>
      <li>A lungtang tuh a kipa, a lau kei ding, amah doute tunga a thudeih tung tuh a muh masiah.</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Israelte Aigupta gam akipan a pawt ua, Jakob inkuanpihte ngei melmak mi lak akipan a pawt lai un.</li>
      <li>Judate tuh a mun siangthou a honghita ua, Israelte tuh a vaihawmna gam mah a honghita uhi.</li>
      <li>Tuipiin huai tuh a mu a, a taimanga; Jordan lui tuh kiksakin a omta hi.</li>
      <li>Tang liante tuh belamtalte bangin a diang ua, mual neute tuh belampa noute bangin.</li>
      <li>Aw nang tuipi, bang na chi a ahia, na taimang tak? Nang Jordan, bang a hi- a ahia, na kik nawntak?</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA aw, kou honpelou in, koumau honpe louin, na min thupina pe jawin, na chitna leh na thutak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Bangachi-a nam chihin, a Pathian uh koia om ahia? Chi uh ahia?</li>
      <li>Ka Pathian u lah van ah a om ngala: a utut a hih ahi.</li>
      <li>A milimte uh dangka leh dangkaeng ahi ua, mihing khutsuak ahi uhi.</li>
      <li>Kam bang a nei ua, lah a pau kei ua; mit bang a nei ua, lah a mu theikei ua:</li>
      <li>Bil bang a nei ua, lah a za theikei ua: nak bang a nei ua, lah gim aza theikei ua;</li>
      <li>Khut bang a nei ua, bangmah lah a khoih theikei ua; khe bang a nei ua, lah a pai theikei ua; a dang un lah a pau thei sam kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Huai bawlte tuh huaite bangin a om ding ua; ahi, huai muang peuhmah te.</li>
      <li>Israelte aw, TOUPA tuh muang un: amah amau panpihpa leh a phaw uh ahi.</li>
      <li>Aron inkuanpihte aw, TOUPA tuh muang un: amah amau panpihpa leh a phaw uh ahi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA laute aw, TOUPA muang un: amau panpihpa leh a phaw uh ahi.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN hon theigige a; vual a jawl ding: Israel inkuanpihte tuh vual a jawl dinga: Aron inkuanpihte tuh vual a jawl ding hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA laute tuh vual a jawl ding, a lian a neuin.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN nou honhihpung deuhdeuh hen, nou leh na tate uh toh.</li>
      <li>TOUPA vualjawlna mute na hi uh, amah tuh lei leh van siampa ahi.</li>
      <li>Vante TOUPA vante ahi a; leilung bel mihing tate kiangah a pia ahi.</li>
      <li>Misiten TOUPA tuh a phat kei ua, mun dai taka pai sukte himhimin lah a phat sam kei uh;Kou bel TOUPA tuh ka phat ta ding uh, tu akipana, khantawnin, TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>
      <li>Kou bel TOUPA tuh ka phat ta ding uh, tu akipana, khantawnin, TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>TOUPA ka it ahi, ka aw leh ka ngetnate a ngaihkhiak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Kei lama a bil a hondoh jiakin ka damsung tengin amah ka sam ding hi.</li>
      <li>Sihna khauhualten honviala, Sheol natnaten honmana: mangbatna leh lungkhamna ka na tuak hi.</li>
      <li>Huaitakin TOUPA min tuh ka lou a: Aw TOUPA, hehpihtakin ka hinna humbitin, chiin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh mi hehpihtheitak leh diktattak ahi a; ahi, i Pathian uh mi lainatthei tak ahi.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN mi mawlte tuh a humbit naka: hihniamin ka oma, aman honhondamta hi.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna aw, na khawlna ah kik nawnta in; TOUPAN lah na tungah hoih takin a hihta ngala.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna sihna lakah, ka mitte khitui lakah, ka khete pukna lakah na humbit ngala.</li>
      <li>Mihing gamah TOUPA maah ka vak ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka gingta a, thu ka gen ding ahi: nakpi taka hihgimin ka om hi.</li>
      <li>Ka lungvaiin, Mi tengteng juau ahi uh, ka na chita mawka.</li>
      <li>Ka tunga a thilhih hoih tengteng jiakin TOUPA kiangah bang ahia ka piak thuk sam ding?</li>
      <li>Hotdamna nou ka la dinga, TOUPA min kalou ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka thuchiamte tuh TOUPA lakah ka tangtun ding, ahi, a mite tengteng maah.</li>
      <li>A mi siangthoute sihna tuh TOUPA theihin manpha pi ahi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na sikha ka hi mahmah hi: na sikha, na sikhanu tapa, ka hi; non henna tuh na sutta hi.</li>
      <li>Kipahthugenna kithoihnate tuh ka honlan dinga, TOUPA min tuh ka lou ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka thuchiamte tuh TOUPA lakah ka tangtun ding, ahi, a mite tengteng maah;TOUPA biakin huangsung intual a h, Jerusalem aw, na laitakah ka tangtun ding hi. TOUPA phat un.</li>
      <li>TOUPA biakin huangsung intual a h, Jerusalem aw, na laitakah ka tangtun ding hi. TOUPA phat un.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>

      <li>Aw, nam chihte aw, TOUPA phat unla; mi chihte aw, amah phat un.A chitna tuh i tunguah a thupiin; TOUPA thutak tuh khantawna om ding a hih jiakin. TOUPA tuh phat un.</li>

      <li>Aw, TOUPA kiangah kipahthu gen un; amah lah a hoih ngala: a chitna leng khantawna om ding a hih jiakin.</li>

      <li>Ka mangbatna akipanin TOUPA tuh ka sama: TOUPAN hondawnga, mun awngthawl ah honomsakta hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh kei lama pang ahi a: ka lau kei ding: mihing in bang a honchih thei dia:</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh kei lama pang honpanpihte laka ahi: huaijiakin hondoute tungah ka thudeihtel tuh ka mu ding hi.</li>

      <li>Mi liante gintak sangin TOUPA a ginna koih tuh a hoihjaw ahi.</li>

      <li>TOUPA khut taklam tuh pahtawiin a om naknaka; TOUPA khut taklamin hang takin a hih naknak hi.</li>
      <li>Ka si kei ding, ka dam ding hi, TOUPA thilhihte tuh ka theisak zo ding.</li>
      <li>TOUPAN nakpi takin honthuzoha: sihna kiangah jaw honpe tel kei hi.</li>
      <li>Diktatna kulh kongkhakte honhonsak un: huaite ah ka lut dinga. TOUPA kiangah kipahthu ka hilh ding hi.</li>
      <li>Hiai tuh TOUPA kongkhak ahi; mi diktatte tuh a lut ding uh.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Lampia mi hoihkimten nuam a sa uhi, TOUPA dan juiten.</li>
      <li>A thutheihsakte juiten nuam a sa uhi, lungtang tengtenga amah zongten.</li>
      <li>A hi, amau diktatlouhna himhim a hih kei ua: a lampite ah a pai jel uhi.</li>
      <li>Nang na thuzohna thute tuh thupiakin non pia a, phatuamngaihtaka ka zuih theihna ding un.</li>
      <li>Aw, na thusehte tuh jui dingin ka omdante hihkipin om leh aw;</li>
      <li>Huai hun chiangin ka zahlak kei dinga, na thupiakte tengteng khawk ka sak hun chiangin.</li>
      <li>Lungtang diktak puin kipahthu ka honhilh ding hi. Na vaihawmna dikte tuh kazil hun chiangin.</li>
      <li>Na thuseh tuh ka jui dinga: aw, honpaisan den ken.</li>
      <li>Valnouin, bangchin ahia a omdan a hihsiangthou ding? Na thu bang jela a omdan venghoihin.</li>
      <li>Ka lungtang tengtengin kon zonga; aw, na thupiakte ka paisan jaw phal mahmah ken.</li>
      <li>Na tunga thil ka hihkhelh louhna dingin na thu tuh ka lungtangah ka kem khawm hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang nuam nasa hi; na thusehte honzil sakin.</li>
      <li>Na kama na vaihawm pawt tengteng ka mukin ka theisakta hi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsak lamah nuam ka saa, hauhsakna tengtenga nuam ka sak bang hialin.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna thute ka ngaihtuah ding a, na lampite ka limsak behlap ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na thuseh tungte khawngah ka kipak dinga: na thu tuh ka mangngilh kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka hin theihna dinginna sikha tungah hoih takinhihin; huchiin na thu ka jui ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na dan thu akipan thillamdang ka muh theihna dingin, ka mitte honhihvaksakin.</li>
      <li>Leiah mikhual ka hi a; na thupiakte ka lakah imken.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna tuh kitam gawpin aoma, chiklai peuha na vaihawmnate a ngaih jiakin.</li>
      <li>Mi kisathei, hamsiat thuakte tuh na taihilha, na thupiakte vakmangsan nakte mahmah.</li>
      <li>Gensiatna leh muhsitna ka kiang akipan la mangin; na thutheihsakte lah ka jui ngala.</li>
      <li>Mi liante leng a tu ua, honkalh ua; himahleh na sikhain na thusehte a ngaihtuah jaw ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte ka kipahna ahi a, thupha honhilh te ahi uh.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna tuh leivuiah a belh bikbeka; na thu bang jelin honhihhalhin.</li>
      <li>Ka omdante ka hontheisaka, nang non dawnga: na thusehte tuh honzil sakin.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna lam tuh hontheisiam sakin: huchiin na thillamdang hih thute ka ngaihtuah ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna lungkham jiakin a tuimang naka: na thu bang jelin honhihhatin.</li>
      <li>Omdan diklou ka kiang akipan lasuan inla; na dan hehpihtakinhonpia in.</li>
      <li>Omdan muanhuai ka tela; na vaihawmnate ka maah ka omsak hi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte ah ka belh chinten a; TOUPA aw, honzahlak sak ken.</li>
      <li>Na thupiak lamah ka tai dinga, ka lungtang na hihlet hun chiangin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na thuseh lampi tuh honensakin; huchiin a tawpphain ka tawn ding hi.</li>
      <li>Theihsiamna honpia in, huchiin, na dan tuh ka kem hoih ding hi, ahi, ka lungtang tengtengin ka jui ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na thupiak lampi-ah honpai sakin, huaiah ka kipak ngala.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsak lamah ka lungtang kihei sakin, huaihamna lamah hi louin.</li>
      <li>Thil bangmahlou phet enlou dingin ka mit kaihei inla, na lampite ah honhihhalhin.</li>
      <li>Na thu tuh na sikha kiangah hihkipin, huai tuh nangmah launa ahi.</li>
      <li>Keia dia gensiatna ka kihtak tuh la mangin; na vaihawmte lah a hoih ngala.</li>
      <li>Ngaiin, na thuzohna thute tuh theih ka ut gigea: na diktatna jiakin honhihhalhin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na chitnate tuh ka kiangah hongpai hen, na hotdamna ngei, na thu bang jelin.</li>
      <li>Huchiin, hon gensete dawnna ding ka nei dinga, na thu lah ka muang ngala.</li>
      <li>Huan, thutak thu tuh ka kam akipan lakhe vek kenla; na vaihawmnate lah ka lamen gige ngala.</li>
      <li>Huchiin na dan ka jui gige dinga, khantawn khantawnin.</li>
      <li>Huan, noplenna ah ka vak dinga; na thuzohna thute lah ka zong ngala.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsak thute kumpipate maah ka gen dinga, ka zum kei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Huan, na thupiak, ka it tungte ah ka kipak ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na thupiak, ka it lamte ah, ka khutte ka jak dinga; na thusehte tuh ka ngaihtuah ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na sikha kianga thuchiam tuh theigigein. Nang non lamet sak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh ka gimthuakna ah leng ka khamuanna ahi: na thuin lah a honhihhalhta ngala.</li>
      <li>Kisatheiten nakpitakin honnuihsan ua: himahleh na dan tuh ka pai hoisan kei hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nidanglaia na vaihawmte ka theigige a, ka kikhamuan jel hi.</li>
      <li>Lunghihlouhnain nakpi takin hon buak khumta a, mi gilousalou-na dan paisante jiakin.</li>
      <li>Ka khualzinna in ah na thusehte ka la ahi ngitnget hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, janchiangin na min ka theigige hi, na dan leng ka jui gige hi.</li>
      <li>Huai tuh ka neia, na thuzohna thute ka vom hoih jiakin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA tuh ka tantuan ahi a: na thu ka jui ding chih ka gen khinta hi.</li>
      <li>Ka lungtang tengtengin na hehpihna ka ngena: na thu bang jelin honhehpihin.</li>
      <li>Ka omdante ka ngaihtuaha, na thutheihsak lamah ka kalsuan hi.</li>
      <li>Ka kintata, na thupiakte jui dingin ka zekai kei hi;</li>
      <li>Mi gilou-salou khauhualten hongak lom gigea; himahleh na dan tuh ka mangngilh kei hi.</li>
      <li>Jan laiin kipahthu honhilh dingin ka thou dinga, na vaihawm diktatte jiakin.</li>
      <li>Nangmah laute tengteng leh na thuzohna thute juite lawm ka hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, leilung na chitnain a dim ahi: na thusehte honhilhin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na thu bangin na sikha tuh na hihhoih jel hi.</li>
      <li>Ngaihtuah siamna leh theihna honhilhin; na thupiakte lah ka gingta ngala.</li>
      <li>Hihhaksate ka om main ka vakmang naka: tunjaw na thu ka juita hi.</li>
      <li>Nang na hoiha, thil hoih leng na hiha: na thusehte honhilhin.</li>
      <li>Kisatheiten ka tungah juau a phuaktawm ua: ka lungtang tengtengin na thuzohna thute tuh ka vom hoih ding hi.</li>

      <li>Na thusehte ka zil theihna dinga hihhaksata ka na om a hoih hi.</li>
      <li>Dangkaeng leh dangka sang tampi sangin na kama dan pawt keia ding a hoihjaw hi.</li>
      <li>Na khutin honsiamin, honsek ahi: na thupiakte ka zil theihna dingin theihsiamna honpiain.</li>

      <li>Ka hin theihna dingin na chitnate ka kiangah hongpai hen: na dan tuh ka kipahna ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Kisathei zahlakin om uhen; dikloupiin honhihniamta ngal ua: himahleh na thuzohna thute ka ngaihtuah ding hi.</li>
      <li>Nang honlaute keilam hongnga uhen, na thutheihsakte a thei ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Ka zahlak louhna dingin ka lungtang na thusehte ah hoihkimin om hen.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna na hotdamna ngaiin a baha: himahleh na thu ka lamen gige hi.</li>

      <li>Meikhu uk savun thawl bang ka nahita ngala; himahleh na thusehte ka mangngilh kei hi.</li>

      <li>Mi kisathei, na dan banga om louten ka kiakna dingin kokhukte bang a tou ua.</li>
      <li>Na thupiak tengteng a ginom ahi: amau diklou piin honsimmoh nak uh; honpanpihin.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh leiah na honhihmang dekdek ua; himahleh na thuzohna thute lah ka kiheisan ngal kei hi.</li>
      <li>Na chitna bang jelin honhihhalhin: huan, na kama thutheihsak ka jui ding hi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, khantawn adingin na thu tuh van ah kiptakin a om hi.</li>
      <li>Na ginomna suan tengteng phain a om ding hi: leilung na hihkipa, a om gige hi.</li>
      <li>Huaite tuh tuiin na vaihawmte bangin a om gige a thil tengteng lah na sikhate ahi ngal ua.</li>
      <li>Na dan ka kipahna hi kei lejaw, ka gimthuakna a mangthangta ding hi inga.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna thute tuh chikpeuhin leng ka mangngilh kei ding: nang lah huaitein nonhilhhalhta ngala.</li>
      <li>Nanga ka hi, honhondamin; na thuzohna thute lah ka zong ngala.</li>
      <li>Mi gilou-salouten honhihmang tumin honngak nak ua; himahleh na thutheihsakte ka ngaihtuah ding hi.</li>
      <li>Hoihkimna tengteng tawpna ka muta; na thupiak tuh a za ngei e.</li>
      <li>Aw, na dan deih hi natel ing e! nituma ka ngaihtuah nak tuh ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thupiakten hondoute sanga piljaw in honbawla; khantawna ka kianga a om gige nak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Honhilhte tengteng sangin pilna ka nei jaw ahi; na thutheihsakte ka ngaihtuah a hih nak jiakin.</li>
      <li>Tekte sangin ka theisiam jaw ahi, na thuzohna thute ka vom hoih jiakin.</li>
      <li>Na thu ka zuih theihna dingin lampi gilou himhim ah ka khete a kalsuan ka phal kei hi.</li>
      <li>Na vaihawmna lak apat ka pial kei; nang non hilh jiakin.</li>
      <li>Na thute ka kama dingin khum hina tele! ahi, ka kama dingin khuaiju sangin a khumjaw hi.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna thute jiakin theihsiamna ka nei jel: huaijiakin omdan diklou peuhmah ka hua hi.</li>
      <li>Na thu tuh ka khe adingin khawnvak ahi a, ka lampi adingin vakna ahi.</li>
      <li>Na vaihawmna diktatte jui dingin ka kichiama, ka hihkip lai hi.</li>
      <li>Nakpi taka hihhaksatin ka oma; TOUPA aw, na thubang jelin honhihhalhin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, hehpih takin ka kam deihthu-a thilpiakte na sang inla, na vaihawmnate honhilhin.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna ka khut ah a om naknaka; himahleh, na dan ka mangngilh ngeikei hi.</li>
      <li>Migilou-salouten ka awkna dingin thang a kam ua; himahleh na thuzohna thute ka vakmang san kei hi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte khantawna gouluah din ka la a; ka lungtang hihnuampen ahi ngala:</li>
      <li>Khantawnin, a tawp phain, na thusehte banga hih dingin ka lungtang ka hoihsak hi.</li>
      <li>Lungsim kiplou neite ka hua a: Na dan tuh ka deih ahi.</li>
      <li>Nang ka bukna mun leh ka phaw na hi a; na thu ka lamet ahi.</li>
      <li>Nou thil hoihlou hihte aw, hongpaisan un; ka Pathian thilpiakte ka vom hoih theihna dingin.</li>
      <li>Ka hin theihna dingin na thu bang jelin honlen nilouh inla, ka lamet tungah zahlakin honomsak ken.</li>
      <li>Honkaiin, huchiin ka bit dinga, na thusehte ka khawksa gige ding ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thusehte vakmang sante tengteng na musita; a khemna ulah juau ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Leia mi gilou-salou tengteng banghiam ek sia bangin a hihmang jela: huaijiakin na thutheihsakte ka deih ahi.</li>
      <li>Ka sa nangmah lauin a linga: na vaihawmnate leng ka lau hi.</li>
      <li>Vai ka hawma, diktakin ka hih jel ahi: honnuaisiahte lakah honngeingaih lou ken.</li>
      <li>Na sikha tungtang thu ah, a hoihna a bultum in: kisatheiten honnuaisiah kei uhen.</li>
      <li>Na hotdamna etnain ka mit a vaikhinta a, na thu diktat tak etna tohin.</li>
      <li>Na chitna bang jelin na sikha tungah hih inla, na thusehte honhilh in.</li>
      <li>Na sikha ka hi a, theihsiamna honpia in; na thutheihsakte ka theihna dingin.</li>
      <li>TOUPA, sep a hunta; na dan bangmahlouin a bawlta ngal ua.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin na thupiakte dangkaeng sangin ka deih ahi; ahi, dangkaeng siangthou sangin leng.</li>
      <li>Huaijiakin thil peuhmah thu-a na thuzohna thu tengteng tuh dikin ka theia; omdan dikou peuhmah ka hua ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte a lamdang ahi: huaijiakin ka hinnain a vom hoih gige a.</li>
      <li>Na thu hilhchetin mite a hihvaka: mi mawlte a theisiam sak jel hi.</li>
      <li>Ka kam zapiin ka kaa, ka ha hawphawpa: na thupiakte ka lunggulh jiakin.</li>
      <li>Kei lam honga inla, honhehpih in, na min deihte na hehpih bangin.</li>
      <li>Ka khe kalsuante na thu-ah hihkip inla; gitlouhna himhim ka tungah thu neisak ken.</li>
      <li>Mihing nuaisiahna lakah honhumbit in; huchiin na thuzohna thute ka jui ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na melin na sikha sunvak inla; na thusehte honhilhin.</li>
      <li>Ka khitui lui tui bangin a luang khia a, na dan a zuih louh jiakun.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang na dika, na vaihawmte leng a dik ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte tuh diktat tak leh ginom mahmahin thu na piaa.</li>
      <li>Ka phattuamngaih nain honhih mangthangta, hondouten na thu a mangngilhtak jiakun.</li>
      <li>Na thu sianthou mahmah ahi; huaijiakin na sikhain a deih hi.</li>
      <li>Mi neu leh mi muhsit ka hi a: himahleh na thuzohna thute ka mangngilh ngeikei hi.</li>
      <li>Na diktatna khantawn diktatna ding ahi a, na dan leng thutak ahi.</li>
      <li>Mangbatna leh lunglaunain hon buak khumta a; himahleh na thupiakte tuh ka kipahna ahi.</li>
      <li>Na thutheihsakte khantawn adingin a dik ahi: theihsiamna honpia in, huchiin, ka hing gige ding hi.</li>
      <li>Ka lungtang tengtengin kon sama; TOUPA aw, hondawng in: na thusehte ka kem hoih ding hi.</li>
      <li>Kon sam jela; hondawng in, huchiin na thutheihsakte ka jui ding hi.</li>
      <li>Phalvak main ka thou-a, huhna deihin ka kikou-a; na thute ka lamen hi.</li>
      <li>Na thu ka ngaihtuah theihna dingin jan vente main, ka mitte a hak uhi.</li>
      <li>Na chitna bang jelin ka aw ngaikhia inla; TOUPA aw, na vaihawmnate bang jelin honhihhalh in.</li>
      <li>Ngaihtuah gilou delhten a honnaih ua: amau jaw na dan gamlata om ahi uhi.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, nang jaw na naia; na thupiak tengteng thutak ahi.</li>
      <li>Nidanglaiin, na thutheihsakte akipanin, huaite khantawn adinginna hihkip chih ka na theita hi.</li>
      <li>Ka haksatna ngaihtuah inla, honhumbit in; na dan lah ka mangngilh ngei ngal keia;</li>
      <li>Ka thu hon genpih inla, hontan in na thu bang jelin honhihhalh in.</li>
      <li>Hotdamna tuh mi gilou-saloute lakah a gamla ahi: na thusehte a zuih louh jiakun.</li>
      <li>TOUPA aw, na chitnate tuh a thupi ahi; na vaihawmnate bang jelin honhihhalh in.</li>
      <li>Honsimmohte leh hondoute tampi ahi ua, himahleh na thutheihsakte ka pai kawi san kei hi.</li>
      <li>Lepchiah taka hihte ka ena, ka lungkim kei hi; na thu a zuih louh jiakun.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna thute ka deihdan ngaihtuah inla, TOUPA aw, na chitna bangbangin honhihhalh in.</li>
      <li>Na thu kigawmkhawm tuh thutak ahi a; na vaihawmna diktat chiteng leng khantawnin a om nilouh ding hi.</li>
      <li>Mi lianten a jiak omlou in hon simmoh ua: himahleh ka lungtang in na thute ahi, a kihtak.</li>
      <li>Na thu ah nuam kasa a, thil thupipi gallaka mu bangin.</li>
      <li>Juau thu ka huain ka kih a; na dan bel ka deih ahi.</li>
      <li>Ni khatin sagih vei kon phat jel ahi, na vaihawm diktatte jiakin.</li>
      <li>Na dan deihten khamuanna thupitak a nei ua; pukna himhim a neikei uhi.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, na hotdamna ka lamen a, na thupiakte bangin ka hih jel hi.</li>
      <li>Ka hinnain na thutheihsakte a jui gige a: ka deih mahmah hi.</li>
      <li>Na thuzohna thute leh na thutheihsakte thu ka jui jela; ka omdan tengteng na maa om ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, kon sap husa na maah hongnai hen: na thu bangbangin theihsiamna honpia in.</li>
      <li>Hehpih ka ngetna na maah tung hen: na thu bangbangin honhumbitin.</li>
      <li>Ka mukin phatna thu gen hen: nang na thusehte non zilsak jel jiakin.</li>
      <li>Ka leiin na thu phatin lasa hen; na thupiak tengteng diktatna a hih jiakin.</li>
      <li>Na khut thu honpanpih dingin mansain om hen: na thuzohna thute lah ka telta ngala.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, na hotdamna ka lunggulh naka; na dan ka kipahna ahi.</li>
      <li>Ka hinna thu hing hen, huchiin a honphat ding hi; na vaihawmnaten leng honpanpih hen.Belam mang bangin ka vak manga; na sikha zong in; na thupiakte lah ka mangngilh nei ngal keia.</li>
      <li>Belam mang bangin ka vak manga; na sikha zong in; na thupiakte lah ka mangngilh nei ngal keia.</li>
