      <li>Zion la khat honsaksak un, chiin, huaiah sala honpiten lasa dingin honsawl ua, honhihgentheiten lah nuamsa dingin leng honchi ngal nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Mi gam peuhah Toupa la bangchin i sa thei dia?</li>
      <li>Jerusalem aw, ka honmangngilh aleh, ka khut taklamin a thilsiam mangngilh sam hen.</li>
      <li>Kon theihgige kei aleh, ka lei ka dangtawngah belh bikbek hen; ka nopsakna pen sanga Jerusalem ka deih jawk ka leh.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, Jerusalem ni jaw Edom suante tungah a selamin theigige in: a suangphum nangawn leng chimsak un, chimsak un, chite.</li>
      <li>Babulon tanu aw, hihmana om ding; ka tung ua na hih banga honthuk ding tuh kipakin a om ding hi.Na tanu noute honla saka, suangpa satna dia zangpa ding tuh kipak takin a om ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na tanu noute honla saka, suangpa satna dia zangpa ding tuh kipak takin a om ding hi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Na kiangah ka lungtang tengtengin kipahthu ka gen dinga: pathiante maah nangmah phatin la ka sa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na biakin siangthou lam ngain chibai ka honbuk dia, na chitna leh na thutak jiakin na min ka phat ding: na thu tuh na min mawngmawng sangin na hihlianta ngala.</li>
      <li>Kon sap niin nang non dawnga, ka hinna hihhatin non hasuana.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, leia kumpipate tengtengin kipahthu a honhilh ding ua, na kama thupawtte lah a zata ngal ua.</li>
      <li>A hi, Toupa omdan thute lain a sa ding ua: Toupa thupidan lah a thupi ngala.</li>
      <li>Toupa tungnungtak ahi naa, mi neute a limsak jel hi: mi kisatheite bel gamlapi akipanin a thei hi.</li>
      <li>Mangbatna lakah vak mahleng leng nang non hihhalh ding; hondoute heh sual dingin na khut na jak dinga, na khut taklam in non hondam ding hi.Toupan ka tungtanga a hih ding tuh a tangtun ding hi: Toupa aw, na chitna tuh khantawnin a om dinga; nangmah khut thilhihte tawpsan ken.</li>
      <li>Toupan ka tungtanga a hih ding tuh a tangtun ding hi: Toupa aw, na chitna tuh khantawnin a om dinga; nangmah khut thilhihte tawpsan ken.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa aw, nang ngentel takin non ensuaka, non theita hi.</li>
      <li>Nang ka tut leh ka din na thei naknaka, ka ngaihtuahna tuh gamlapi akipanin leng na thei thei hi.</li>
      <li>Ka pai leh ka lup non entel jela, ka omdan tengteng na thei vek hi.</li>
      <li>Ngaiin, Toupa aw, nang na theih siang vek louh, ka lei ah thu himhim a om kei hi.</li>
      <li>Nang ka nunglam leh ka mallamah non umsuaka, ka tungah na khut na koih lai hi.</li>
      <li>Huchitela theihna kei dingin a lamdang lua a; a sang tela, ka pha zou kei hi.</li>
      <li>Na kha kiang akipanin koiah ka pai dia? Na ma akipan koiah ka tai mang dia?</li>
      <li>Van ah kahtou ning chileng, huaiah lah na om ngala: Sheol ah lupna bawl ning chileng ngaiin, huaiah leng na om jel ngala.</li>
      <li>Jing kha jakin, tuipi tawp pekah vaom ning chi leng;</li>
      <li>Huaiah leng na khutin non pi dinga, na khut taklamin honlen ding ahi ngala.</li>
      <li>Pellouin mialin honkhuh zouvek ding a, ka kima vak tuh jan ahi ding chi dek lengleng;</li>
      <li>Mialin leng nang lakah bangmah a liah keia, jan lah sun bangin a vakjaw ahi: nang dingin mial leh vak a kibang salpsap hi.</li>
      <li>Nangmah ngeiin ka lungsim na neia: ka nu gilsungah non phankhawm hi.</li>
      <li>Na kiangah kipahthu kon hilh dinga; lauhuai tak leh lamdang pi-a bawl ka hih jiakin: na thilhihte lah lamdang tak ahi a; huai tuh ka hinnain a theitel mahmah hi.</li>
      <li>A guka bawla ka oma, lei mun nuainungpena kilawmtaka bawla ka om laiin, ka guh ka tang nang lakah selin a om kei hi.</li>
      <li>Ka lim kibawl kim nailou tuh na mitin a mu-a, na laibu ah ka hiangte tengteng gelh vek ahi, ani sima bawlin a om jela, khat leng a om nai louh laiin.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, na ngaihtuahnate kei adingin manpha hina tele! a gawmkhawmna thupi hina tele!</li>
      <li>Sim dek mahleng, a tamdan tuh piaunel sangin a tam zo ding: ka khanloh aleh, na kiangah ka om nilouh naknak ahi.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, mi gilou-saloute na thah ngei dinga; huchiin sisan suah hat miten honpaisan ding.</li>
      <li>Amau tuh gilou takin nang a hon gensia un, nangmah douten na min tuh a genthanghuai nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, nangmah hote ka ho kei ahia? Nangmah sualte tungah ka lung kim lou kei ahia?</li>
      <li>Amau tuh huat petmahin ka huaa: hondoute dingin ka sep chiat hi.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, ngentel takin honen suak inla, ka lungtang thei in: honchian inla, ka ngaihtuahnate thei in.Huan, kei ah gilou-salou lam mawngmawng a om hiam om lou, en inla, khantawn lampi ah honpi in.</li>
      <li>Huan, kei ah gilou-salou lam mawngmawng a om hiam om lou, en inla, khantawn lampi ah honpi in.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa aw, mi gilou lakah honhumbit inla; mi ngongtat lakah honhum in:</li>
      <li>Amau tuh a lungtang uah thilhihkhelhte a ngaihtuah ua: dou dingin a kikhawm gige uhi.</li>
      <li>A lei uh gul bangin ahiamsak ua; a neh sung uah thangtom gu a om hi. Selah.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, mi gilou-salou khut lakah honkem hoih inla; mi ngongtat lakah honhum in: amau tuh ka khe kalsuante sawnkawi a tum uhi.</li>
      <li>Mi kisatheiten ka awkna dingin thang a guk kam ua, khauhualte toh; lam sikah len a phah ua; ka awkna dingin thangte a kam uhi. Selah.</li>
      <li>Toupa kiangah, nang jaw ka Pathian na hi: Toupa aw, hehpih ka nget awte na bil na doh in.</li>
      <li>Toupa Pathian aw, non hotdamna hihhatpa aw, nang kisual ni chiah ka lu non khuhsaka.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, mi gilou-salou deihlamte jaw phal kenla; a ngaihtuahna gilou tuh piching sak ken; huchi kei leh a kipahtawi kha ding uhi, ka chia. Selah.</li>
      <li>Honumsuakte lu tuh, amau muka thugilou a gen un khuh hen.</li>
      <li>Meiamte a tunguah kia henla: meia paihin om uhenla; a thoh tak louhna ding un kokhuk thupi takah paihin om uhen.</li>
      <li>Thu hoihlou genpa tuh lei ah hihkipin a om kei dinga: mi ngongtat hihse dingin thil hoihlouin a zong ding hi.</li>
      <li>Toupan gim thuakte a thu uah a gum ding chih ka thei, tagahte adin diktakin vai a hawm ding.Pellouin mi diktatten na min maah a om ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Pellouin mi diktatten na min maah a om ding uhi.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa, kon sam hi, ka kiangah hongpai meng inla: kon sapin ka aw ah bil na dohin.</li>

      <li>Toupa aw, ka kam bulah vengmi tusak inla; ka muk kongkhak veng in.</li>
      <li>Gilou-salou thilte thilhihkhial mite hihpih dingin, ka lungtang thil hoihlou himhim lamah kiheksak kenla; a neklimte uh honen sak ken.</li>
      <li>Mi diktatin honsat hen, migitna ahi ding; hontaihilh hen; himahleh migilouten ka lu thaunilh ngei kei hen, a nasep giloute uh huain ka thum gige ngala.</li>
      <li>Amau mohpaih dingte kianga piakkhiak a hih chiangin, Toupa thu a dik chih a thei ding uh.</li>
      <li>Min lei a leha a hihjan bangin a guhte uh hankoutangah hihdalhin a om ding.</li>
      <li>Toupa Pathian aw, ka mitin nang lam lah a en ngal naka: nangmah ah ka muanna ka nga gige; ka hinna tuh vuaktangin nuse ken.</li>
      <li>Ka awkna dinga thang a kam lak uah honhum in, thilhihkhialte thang lakah te toh.Ken ka khen laiin, migilou-salou tuh amau len ah te khawng kelut uhen.</li>

      <li>Ka kha ka sunga a bahlaiin, nangmah ngaiin ka lampi na theia. Ka paina lampi-ah ka awkna dingin thang a guk kam uhi.</li>
      <li>Ka taklamah om inla, en dih, kuamah honthei himhim a omta kei ua; ka kihumbitna a omta keia; kuamah himhimin ka hinna a limsakta kei uhi.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, kon sama; nang ka kihumbitna, mihing gama ka tantuam na hi, ka chi a.</li>
      <li>Ka kikou husa ngaikhia in; nakpi taka hihniamin ka omta ngala. Honsimmohte lakah honhumbit in; kei sangin a hat zo ngalua.Na min ka phat theihna dingin, ka hinna suangkulh akipanin pi khia in: mi diktatten honum suak ding ua; nang hoihtaka non hih ding jiakin.</li>
      <li>Na min ka phat theihna dingin, ka hinna suangkulh akipanin pi khia in: mi diktatten honum suak ding ua; nang hoihtaka non hih ding jiakin.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa aw, ka thumna ngaikhia inla; hehpih ka ngetna ah bil doh inla; na giomna jiak leh na jiakin hondawng in.</li>
      <li>Na sikha tungah vaihawm ken; na mitmuh ah mihing himhim siamtang a om ding lah a om ngal kei ua.</li>
      <li>Melmain lah ka hinna a simmoh ngala; ka hinna tuh leiah a sat puka: sawtpi-a sisate bangin, mun mial takte ah honomsak hi.</li>

      <li>Jingsangin na chitna thu hontheisak in; nang lah kon muang ngala; ka paina ding lampi hontheisak in; ka lungsim lah na kiangah ka koih kip jel ngala.</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Toupa ka suangpa tuh phatin om hen, aman ka khutte galkap a zilsak jela, ka khutzungte dou dingin a chil jel hi.</li>
      <li>Ka chitna leh ka kulhpi, ka insang leh honhumbitpa, ka phaw leh ka muanna ngakna ka nuaia ka mite zoujelpa ahi.</li>
      <li>Toupa mihing kua ahia a hiha, na theih naknak? Mihing tapa leng kua ahia a hiha, na ngaihtuah naknak?</li>
      <li>Mihing jaw bangmahlou bang lel ahi a: a damsung nite lim mang jel bang ahi.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, na vante kunsakin hongpai suk inla: tangte koih in, huchiin a khukhe ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Khua phesak inla, amau tuh dalhsakin: na thalte tuh kap khia inla, hihbuai gawp in.</li>
      <li>Tunglam akipanin na khutin honsawk inla; honhonkhia inla, tuilian akipanin:</li>
      <li>A kam un bangmahlou peuh a gen ua, a khut taklam utuh khut taklam diklou ahi.</li>
      <li>Pathian aw, nangmah pahtawiin la thak ka sa dinga: pekging gui sawm nei toh nangmah phatin la ka sa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Amah ahi, kumpipate kianga hotdamna piaa, namsau mi hihsethei laka a sikha David honkhepa pen.</li>
      <li>Honhonkhia inla, mikhualte khut akipan honhumbit in, a kam un thu bangmahlou peuh a gen nak ua, a khut taklam uh khuttaklam diklou ahi.</li>
      <li>Ka tate uh a hongvalnou ua sing nou didip banga a om ua; ka tanute u leng inpi omdan gel banga a ninga suangkhuak banga a om hun un;</li>
      <li>Ka buhinte uh a dima, thil chichih a om phetphuta; ka belamte un leng nou a sang asanga tam. A sing asinga tam ka mun ua a neih chiang un;</li>
      <li>Ka bawngte uh a hongsuan phata; nou neihsiat himhim a pmlouha; insungloh himhim leh pawtkhia himhim a omlouha, ka konhzingte ua kikou husa himhim a om louh chiangin;Huchibanga om mite tuh kipak takin a om nak uhi: ahi, Toupa Pathian a nei mite tuh kipak takin a om nak uhi.</li>
      <li>Huchibanga om mite tuh kipak takin a om nak uhi: ahi, Toupa Pathian a nei mite tuh kipak takin a om nak uhi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumpipa aw, ka Pathian, kon pahtawi dinga; na min khantawn khantawnin ka phat ding hi.</li>
      <li>Nitengin kon phat dinga; na min khantawn khantawnin ka phat ding hi.</li>
      <li>Toupa tuh a thupi-a, nakpi taka phat ding ahi; a thupidan tuh suikhiak vual ahi kei hi.</li>
      <li>Suan khatin suandang kiangah na thilhihte tuh a phat sawnsawn ding ua, na thilhih thupitakte tuh a theisak ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Nangmah pahtawina kilawmdan thupitak lehm na thillamdang-hihte ka ngaihtuah ding hi.</li>
      <li>Miten na thilhih mulkimhuaitakte hatdan a gen ding ua; ken leng na thupidan ka theisak sam ding hi.</li>
      <li>Na hoihna thupitak a theih uh a gen ding ua, na diktatna tuh nuamsa takin lain a sa ding uhi.</li>
      <li>Toupa mi hehpihthei, chitnaa dim; lungnel, chitna thupitak nei ahi.</li>
      <li>Toupa bangkim tungah leng a hoih ahi; a chitnate tuh a thilsiam tengteng tungah a oma.</li>
      <li>Toupa aw, na thilsiam tengtengin na kiangah kipahthu a honhilh ding ua; misiangthouten leng nang a hon phat ding uhi.</li>

      <li>Mihing tate kianga a thilhih thupitakte leh, a gam kilawmna thupidan theisak dingin.</li>
      <li>Na gam tuh khantawn gam ding ahi a, na thu neihna tuh suan omsung tengtengin a om gige ding hi. Toupa tuh a thute ah a muanhuaia, a nasepte ah deihsak a siam hi.</li>
      <li>Toupan pukte tengteng a len gige jela, kun kheukheua om tengteng a kaitang jel hi.</li>
      <li>Amau tengteng mit tuh nang tungah a tu a; a hun takah a annek ding uh na pia hi;</li>
      <li>Na khut na jaka, thil hing teng deih tuh na hihtaisak hi.</li>
      <li>Toupa tuh a lampi tengteng a dika, a nasep peuhmah mi hehpihthei ahi.</li>
      <li>Toupa tuh amah minlou tengteng kiangah a nai hi, thudika amah lou peuhmahte kiangah.</li>
      <li>Amah laute deihlam tuh a hihtangtung dinga; a kahna uh leng a za dinga, amau tuh a hondam ding hi.</li>
      <li>Amah itte tengteng tuh Toupan a hawia; Ahihhangin migilou tuh a hihmangthang ding hi.Toupa phatna tuh ka kamin a gen dinga; huan sa peuhmahin a min siangthou tuh khantawn khantawnin phat uhen!</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa phat un! Ka hinna aw, Toupa phat in.</li>
      <li>Ka damsung tengin Toupa ka phat dinga; ka hin laitengin ka Pathian phatin la ka sa ding hi.</li>
      <li>Mi liante gingta kei unla, mihing tapa panpihna himhim omlouhna, gingta sam kei un.</li>
      <li>A naknain a pawtsana, amah tuh lei ah a kik nawna; huai ni mahin a ngaihtuahnate tuh a mang pah ahi.</li>
      <li>Jakob Pathian a panpih dia nei miin nuam a sa hi, a lametna tuh Toupa a Pathian ah a om:</li>
      <li>Aman van leh lei a bawla, tuipi leh a sunga om tengteng, aman tuh thudik a vom gige hi.</li>
      <li>Nuaisiaha omte adinga vai a hawm saka, gilkialte kiangah an a pia. Hentate Toupan a suaktasak hi;</li>
      <li>Toupan mittawte mit a hihvak saka; kun kheukheute Toupan a kaitanga; Toupan mi diktatte a it hi;</li>
      <li>Toupan mikhualte a venga; nu-bei-pabeite leh meithaite a khotuaha; ahihhangin migiloute lampi a lumlehsak hi.Toupan khantawnin vai a hawm ding. Zion aw, na Pathianin, suanteng tanin. Toupa phat un!</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Toupa phat un! I Pathian phata lasak a hoih ngal; amah jaw mi deihsak a siama, phat a kilawm him ahi.</li>
      <li>Toupan Jerusalem a dingsak nawna; Israel delh khiakte a pi khawm nawn hi.</li>
      <li>Khasiate a hihdama, a liamnate utuh a tuam jel hi.</li>
      <li>Aksi tamdan a sima; a min uh a sa chiat jel hi.</li>
      <li>I Toupa a thu[i-a. thilhihtheihna lamah leng hattak ahi; a pilnain tawpin a neikei ding hi.</li>
      <li>Toupan thunuailutte a len gige a; mi gilou-saloute leiah a hihniam jel hi.</li>
      <li>Kipahthugena Toupa pahtawiin lasa unla; kaihging toh I Pathian phatin lasa un</li>
      <li>Aman van meipi a khuhsaka, lei adingin vuah a sutuaha, tangte ah loupa a pousak hi.</li>
      <li>Aman sa kiangah a nekding uh a pe jela, va-aknou hamhamte kiangah toh.</li>
      <li>Aman tuh sakol hatna tungah a kipak keia; mihing khe tungte ah leng kipahna himhim a neikei naknak hi.</li>
      <li>Toupan amah laute tungah kipahna a nei jela, a chitna lamente tungah.</li>
      <li>Jerusalem aw, Toupa phat un; Zion aw, na Pathian phat in.</li>
      <li>Aman na kulh kongkhakte kalhna sing tawnte a khauhsaka; na sunga na tate om lah vual a jawl ngala.</li>
      <li>Na gamgi singah lemna a siama; buh hoihpen chiin a honhihdim jel ahi.</li>
      <li>A thupiak tuh leiah a sawl khiaa: a thu tuh hattakin a tai hi.</li>
      <li>Vukju tuh belam mul bangin a pia a; vuk kia vut bangin a theh jak hi.</li>
      <li>A tui khal tuh tanghou them nen bangin a paikhia: amah votna maah kua ahia ding thei ding?</li>
      <li>A thu a sawl khiaa, huaite tuh a huih a nungsaka, huchiin tuite a hongluang jel hi.</li>
      <li>A thu tuh Jakobte kiangah a langsaka, a thusehte leh a vaihawmte leng Israelte kiangah a langsak jel hi.Aman kua nam tungah mah huchi bangin a hih ngeikeia; a vaihawmte lah a thei sam kei uhi. Toupa tuh phat un!</li>

    <ol>
      <li>Toupa phat un! Van akipante Toupa phat unla: tunglamahte khawng amah phat un.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa phat un! Toupa pahtawiin la thak sa unla, mi siangthoute kikhopna ah a phatna lasa un.</li>
      <li>Israelte tuh amau siampa tungah kipak uhenla; Zion tate a kumpipa u tungah nuam uhen.</li>
      <li>A min tuh louin phst ehenla; khuangta leh kaihging toh amah phatin lasa uhen.</li>
      <li>Toupa lah a mite tungah a kipak ngal naka; thunuailutte tuh hotdamnain a jem ding hi.</li>
      <li>Mi siangthoute tuh thupina ah kipak takin om uhenla: a lupna tunguahte nuamin lasa uhen!</li>
      <li>Pathian pahtawia phatna tuh a kam uah om henla, namsau hiam tuah a khut uah leng om hen.</li>
      <li>Nam chih tunga phu laa, mi chih tunga gawtna tungsak ding leh,</li>
      <li>A kumpipate uh khainianga hena, a mi hoihte uh sikkolte bunsak ding lehVaihawm gelhkhiaksaa a tung ua thulel dingin: huai kilawmna tuh a mi siangthou tengtengin a nei chiat ua. Toupa tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>Vaihawm gelhkhiaksaa a tung ua thulel dingin: huai kilawmna tuh a mi siangthou tengtengin a nei chiat ua. Toupa tuh phat un!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Toupa phat un! Pathian a mun siangthou ah phat unla: a thilhihtheihna huihkhua zapi-ah amah tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>A thilhih thupitakte jiakin amah tuh phat unla: a thupi mahmah dan bang jelin amah tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>Pengkul ging in amah phat unla: pekging leh kaihgingin amah phat un!</li>
      <li>Khuangta leh lamin amah phat unla: kaihging chi tuamtuam leh tamngaiin amah tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>Dakkhutbet ngaihtakin amah phat unla; dakkhutbet ngaihtakin amah phat un!Bangkim, ha thei peuhmahin Toupa phat hen! Toupa tuh phat un!</li>
      <li>Bangkim, ha thei peuhmahin Toupa phat hen! Toupa tuh phat un!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
</ol>
